# React Router API Reference

React Router API Reference
==========================

[![npm package](https://img.shields.io/npm/v/react-router-dom.svg?style=flat-square)](https://www.npmjs.org/package/react-router-dom)
 [![build](https://img.shields.io/github/actions/workflow/status/remix-run/react-router/test.yml?branch=dev&style=square)](https://github.com/remix-run/react-router/actions/workflows/test.yml)

React Router is a multi-strategy router for React bridging the gap from React 18 to React 19. You can use it maximally as a React framework or minimally as a library with your own architecture.

*   [Getting Started - Framework](https://reactrouter.com/start/framework/installation)
    
*   [Getting Started - Library](https://reactrouter.com/start/library/installation)
    
*   [Upgrade from v6](https://reactrouter.com/upgrading/v6)
    
*   [Upgrade from Remix](https://reactrouter.com/upgrading/remix)
    
*   [Changelog](https://github.com/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/CHANGELOG.md)
    

Packages[](#md:packages)

-------------------------

*   [react-router](./modules/react_router)
    
*   [@react-router/dev](./modules/_react_router_dev)
    
*   [@react-router/node](./modules/_react_router_node)
    
*   [@react-router/cloudflare](./modules/_react_router_cloudflare)
    
*   [@react-router/serve](./modules/_react_router_serve)
    
*   [@react-router/fs-routes](./modules/_react_router_fs_routes)
    

Previous Versions[](#md:previous-versions)

-------------------------------------------

*   [v6](https://reactrouter.com/v6)
    
*   [v5](https://v5.reactrouter.com/)
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

# NavigationType | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [NavigationType](react_router.NavigationType.html)
    

Enumeration NavigationType
==========================

Actions represent the type of change to a location value.

##### Index

### Enumeration Members

[Pop](react_router.NavigationType.html#Pop)
 [Push](react_router.NavigationType.html#Push)
 [Replace](react_router.NavigationType.html#Replace)

Enumeration Members
-------------------

### Pop[](#Pop)

Pop

A POP indicates a change to an arbitrary index in the history stack, such as a back or forward navigation. It does not describe the direction of the navigation, only that the current index changed.

Note: This is the default action for newly created history objects.

### Push[](#Push)

Push

A PUSH indicates a new entry being added to the history stack, such as when a link is clicked and a new page loads. When this happens, all subsequent entries in the stack are lost.

### Replace[](#Replace)

Replace

A REPLACE indicates the entry at the current index in the history stack being replaced by a new one.

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

### On This Page

Enumeration Members

[Pop](#Pop)
[Push](#Push)
[Replace](#Replace)

---

Properties

### context[](#context)

context: unknown

If using the new style context, re-declare this in your class to be the `React.ContextType` of your `static contextType`. Should be used with type annotation or static contextType.

    static contextType = MyContext// For TS pre-3.7:context!: React.ContextType<typeof MyContext>// For TS 3.7 and above:declare context: React.ContextType<typeof MyContext>
    

#### See[](#See)

[https://react.dev/reference/react/Component#context](https://react.dev/reference/react/Component#context)

### `Static` `Optional`contextType[](#contextType)

contextType?: Context<any\>

If set, `this.context` will be set at runtime to the current value of the given Context.

Usage:

    type MyContext = numberconst Ctx = React.createContext<MyContext>(0)class Foo extends React.Component {  static contextType = Ctx  context!: React.ContextType<typeof Ctx>  render () {    return <>My context's value: {this.context}</>;  }}
    

#### See[](#See-1)

[https://react.dev/reference/react/Component#static-contexttype](https://react.dev/reference/react/Component#static-contexttype)

### `Optional`componentDidCatch[](#componentDidCatch)

*   componentDidCatch(error, errorInfo): void[](#componentDidCatch.componentDidCatch-1)
    
*   Catches exceptions generated in descendant components. Unhandled exceptions will cause the entire component tree to unmount.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   error: Error
    *   errorInfo: ErrorInfo
    
    #### Returns void
    

### `Optional`componentDidMount[](#componentDidMount)

*   componentDidMount(): void[](#componentDidMount.componentDidMount-1)
    
*   Called immediately after a component is mounted. Setting state here will trigger re-rendering.
    
    #### Returns void
    

### `Optional`componentDidUpdate[](#componentDidUpdate)

*   componentDidUpdate(prevProps, prevState, snapshot?): void[](#componentDidUpdate.componentDidUpdate-1)
    
*   Called immediately after updating occurs. Not called for the initial render.
    
    The snapshot is only present if getSnapshotBeforeUpdate is present and returns non-null.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   prevProps: Readonly<RemixErrorBoundaryProps\>
    *   prevState: Readonly<RemixErrorBoundaryState\>
    *   `Optional`snapshot: any
    
    #### Returns void
    

### `Optional`componentWillMount[](#componentWillMount)

*   componentWillMount(): void[](#componentWillMount.componentWillMount-1)
    
*   Called immediately before mounting occurs, and before `Component#render`. Avoid introducing any side-effects or subscriptions in this method.
    
    Note: the presence of getSnapshotBeforeUpdate or getDerivedStateFromProps prevents this from being invoked.
    
    #### Returns void
    
    #### Deprecated[](#Deprecated-1)
    
    16.3, use componentDidMount or the constructor instead; will stop working in React 17
    
    #### See[](#See-2)
    
    *   [https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#initializing-state](https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#initializing-state)
        
    *   [https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#gradual-migration-path](https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#gradual-migration-path)
        
    

### `Optional`componentWillReceiveProps[](#componentWillReceiveProps)

*   componentWillReceiveProps(nextProps, nextContext): void[](#componentWillReceiveProps.componentWillReceiveProps-1)
    
*   Called when the component may be receiving new props. React may call this even if props have not changed, so be sure to compare new and existing props if you only want to handle changes.
    
    Calling `Component#setState` generally does not trigger this method.
    
    Note: the presence of getSnapshotBeforeUpdate or getDerivedStateFromProps prevents this from being invoked.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   nextProps: Readonly<RemixErrorBoundaryProps\>
    *   nextContext: any
    
    #### Returns void
    
    #### Deprecated[](#Deprecated-2)
    
    16.3, use static getDerivedStateFromProps instead; will stop working in React 17
    
    #### See[](#See-3)
    
    *   [https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#updating-state-based-on-props](https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#updating-state-based-on-props)
        
    *   [https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#gradual-migration-path](https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#gradual-migration-path)

    #### Returns void
    

### `Optional`componentWillUpdate[](#componentWillUpdate)

*   componentWillUpdate(nextProps, nextState, nextContext): void[](#componentWillUpdate.componentWillUpdate-1)

    Note: You cannot call `Component#setState` here.
    
    Note: the presence of getSnapshotBeforeUpdate or getDerivedStateFromProps prevents this from being invoked.
    
    #### Parameters

    *   nextState: Readonly<RemixErrorBoundaryState\>
    *   nextContext: any
    
    #### Returns void

### `Optional`getSnapshotBeforeUpdate[](#getSnapshotBeforeUpdate)

*   getSnapshotBeforeUpdate(prevProps, prevState): any[](#getSnapshotBeforeUpdate.getSnapshotBeforeUpdate-1)
    
*   Runs before React applies the result of `render` to the document, and returns an object to be given to componentDidUpdate. Useful for saving things such as scroll position before `render` causes changes to it.
    
    Note: the presence of getSnapshotBeforeUpdate prevents any of the deprecated lifecycle events from running.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   prevProps: Readonly<RemixErrorBoundaryProps\>
    *   prevState: Readonly<RemixErrorBoundaryState\>
    
    #### Returns any

### `Optional`shouldComponentUpdate[](#shouldComponentUpdate)

*   shouldComponentUpdate(nextProps, nextState, nextContext): boolean[](#shouldComponentUpdate.shouldComponentUpdate-1)
    
*   Called to determine whether the change in props and state should trigger a re-render.
    
    `Component` always returns true. `PureComponent` implements a shallow comparison on props and state and returns true if any props or states have changed.
    
    If false is returned, `Component#render`, `componentWillUpdate` and `componentDidUpdate` will not be called.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   nextProps: Readonly<RemixErrorBoundaryProps\>
    *   nextState: Readonly<RemixErrorBoundaryState\>
    *   nextContext: any
    
    #### Returns boolean
    

### `Optional`UNSAFE\_componentWillMount[](#UNSAFE_componentWillMount)

*   UNSAFE\_componentWillMount(): void[](#UNSAFE_componentWillMount.UNSAFE_componentWillMount-1)
    
*   Called immediately before mounting occurs, and before `Component#render`. Avoid introducing any side-effects or subscriptions in this method.
    
    This method will not stop working in React 17.
    
    Note: the presence of getSnapshotBeforeUpdate or getDerivedStateFromProps prevents this from being invoked.
    
    #### Returns void
    
    #### Deprecated[](#Deprecated-4)
    
    16.3, use componentDidMount or the constructor instead
    
    #### See[](#See-5)
    
    *   [https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#initializing-state](https://legacy.reactjs.org/blog/2018/03/27/update-on-async-rendering.html#initializing-state)

# AppLoadContext | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [AppLoadContext](react_router.AppLoadContext.html)
    

Interface AppLoadContext
========================

An object of unknown type for route loaders and actions provided by the server's `getLoadContext()` function. This is defined as an empty interface specifically so apps can leverage declaration merging to augment this type globally: [https://www.typescriptlang.org/docs/handbook/declaration-merging.html](https://www.typescriptlang.org/docs/handbook/declaration-merging.html)

#### Indexable

*   \[key: string\]: unknown
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

# AwaitProps | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [AwaitProps](react_router.AwaitProps.html)
    

Interface AwaitProps<Resolve>
=============================

interface AwaitProps<[Resolve](react_router.AwaitProps.html#Resolve)
\> {  
    [children](react_router.AwaitProps.html#children)
: ReactNode | AwaitResolveRenderFunction<[Resolve](react_router.AwaitProps.html#Resolve)
\>;  
    [errorElement](react_router.AwaitProps.html#errorElement)
?: ReactNode;  
    [resolve](react_router.AwaitProps.html#resolve-1)
: [Resolve](react_router.AwaitProps.html#Resolve)
;  
}

#### Type Parameters

*   Resolve

##### Index

### Properties

[children](react_router.AwaitProps.html#children)
 [errorElement?](react_router.AwaitProps.html#errorElement)
 [resolve](react_router.AwaitProps.html#resolve-1)

Properties
----------

### children[](#children)

children: ReactNode | AwaitResolveRenderFunction<[Resolve](react_router.AwaitProps.html#Resolve)
\>

When using a function, the resolved value is provided as the parameter.

    <Await resolve={reviewsPromise}>  {(resolvedReviews) => <Reviews items={resolvedReviews} />}</Await>
    

When using React elements, [useAsyncValue](../functions/react_router.useAsyncValue.html)
 will provide the resolved value:

    <Await resolve={reviewsPromise}>  <Reviews /></Await>function Reviews() {  const resolvedReviews = useAsyncValue()  return <div>...</div>}
    

### `Optional`errorElement[](#errorElement)

errorElement?: ReactNode

The error element renders instead of the children when the promise rejects.

    <Await  errorElement={<div>Oops</div>}  resolve={reviewsPromise}>  <Reviews /></Await>
    

To provide a more contextual error, you can use the [useAsyncError](../functions/react_router.useAsyncError.html)
 in a child component

    <Await  errorElement={<ReviewsError />}  resolve={reviewsPromise}>  <Reviews /></Await>function ReviewsError() {  const error = useAsyncError()  return <div>Error loading reviews: {error.message}</div>}
    

If you do not provide an errorElement, the rejected value will bubble up to the nearest route-level [ErrorBoundary](react_router.NonIndexRouteObject.html#ErrorBoundary)
 and be accessible via [useRouteError](../functions/react_router.useRouteError.html)
 hook.

### resolve[](#resolve-1)

resolve: [Resolve](react_router.AwaitProps.html#Resolve)

Takes a promise returned from a [loader](../types/react_router.LoaderFunction.html)
 value to be resolved and rendered.

    import { useLoaderData, Await } from "react-router"
    
    export async function loader() {
      let reviews = getReviews() // not awaited
      let book = await getBook()
      return {
        book,
        reviews, // this is a promise
      }
    }
    
    export default function Book() {
      const {
        book,
        reviews, // this is the same promise
      } = useLoaderData()
    
      return (
        
          {book.title}
          {book.description}
          }>
            
              
            
          
        
      );
    }
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

[errorElement](#errorElement)
[resolve](#resolve-1)

# CookieSerializeOptions | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [CookieSerializeOptions](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html)
    

Interface CookieSerializeOptions
================================

Serialize options.

interface CookieSerializeOptions {  
    [domain](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#domain)
?: string;  
    [encode](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#encode)
?: ((str: string) => string);  
    [expires](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#expires)
?: Date;  
    [httpOnly](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#httpOnly)
?: boolean;  
    [maxAge](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#maxAge)
?: number;  
    [partitioned](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#partitioned)
?: boolean;  
    [path](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#path)
?: string;  
    [priority](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#priority)
?: "high" | "low" | "medium";  
    [sameSite](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#sameSite)
?:  
        | boolean  
        | "none"  
        | "strict"  
        | "lax";  
    [secure](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#secure)
?: boolean;  
}

##### Index

### Properties

[domain?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#domain)
 [encode?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#encode)
 [expires?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#expires)
 [httpOnly?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#httpOnly)
 [maxAge?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#maxAge)
 [partitioned?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#partitioned)
 [path?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#path)
 [priority?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#priority)
 [sameSite?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#sameSite)
 [secure?](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html#secure)

Properties
----------

### `Optional`domain[](#domain)

domain?: string

Specifies the value for the [`Domain` `Set-Cookie` attribute](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-5.2.3)
. When no domain is set clients consider the cookie to apply to the current domain only.

### `Optional`encode[](#encode)

encode?: ((str: string) => string)

Specifies a function that will be used to encode a [cookie-value](https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc6265#section-4.1.1)
. Since value of a cookie has a limited character set (and must be a simple string), this function can be used to encode a value into a string suited for a cookie's value, and should mirror `decode` when parsing.

#### Default[](#Default)

    encodeURIComponent
    

### `Optional`expires[](#expires)

expires?: Date

Specifies the `Date` object to be the value for the [`Expires` `Set-Cookie` attribute](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-5.2.1)
. When no expiration is set clients consider this a "non-persistent cookie" and delete it the current session is over.

The [cookie storage model specification](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-5.3)
 states that if both `expires` and `maxAge` are set, then `maxAge` takes precedence, but it is possible not all clients by obey this, so if both are set, they should point to the same date and time.

### `Optional`httpOnly[](#httpOnly)

httpOnly?: boolean

Enables the [`HttpOnly` `Set-Cookie` attribute](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-5.2.6)
. When enabled, clients will not allow client-side JavaScript to see the cookie in `document.cookie`.

### `Optional`maxAge[](#maxAge)

maxAge?: number

Specifies the `number` (in seconds) to be the value for the [`Max-Age` `Set-Cookie` attribute](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-5.2.2)
.

The [cookie storage model specification](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-5.3)
 states that if both `expires` and `maxAge` are set, then `maxAge` takes precedence, but it is possible not all clients by obey this, so if both are set, they should point to the same date and time.

### `Optional`partitioned[](#partitioned)

partitioned?: boolean

Enables the [`Partitioned` `Set-Cookie` attribute](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-cutler-httpbis-partitioned-cookies/)
. When enabled, clients will only send the cookie back when the current domain _and_ top-level domain matches.

This is an attribute that has not yet been fully standardized, and may change in the future. This also means clients may ignore this attribute until they understand it. More information about can be found in [the proposal](https://github.com/privacycg/CHIPS)
.

### `Optional`path[](#path)

path?: string

Specifies the value for the [`Path` `Set-Cookie` attribute](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-5.2.4)
. When no path is set, the path is considered the ["default path"](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-5.1.4)
.

### `Optional`priority[](#priority)

priority?: "high" | "low" | "medium"

Specifies the value for the [`Priority` `Set-Cookie` attribute](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-west-cookie-priority-00#section-4.1)
.

*   `'low'` will set the `Priority` attribute to `Low`.
*   `'medium'` will set the `Priority` attribute to `Medium`, the default priority when not set.
*   `'high'` will set the `Priority` attribute to `High`.

More information about priority levels can be found in [the specification](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-west-cookie-priority-00#section-4.1)
.

### `Optional`sameSite[](#sameSite)

sameSite?:  
    | boolean  
    | "none"  
    | "strict"  
    | "lax"

Specifies the value for the [`SameSite` `Set-Cookie` attribute](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-ietf-httpbis-rfc6265bis-09#section-5.4.7)
.

*   `true` will set the `SameSite` attribute to `Strict` for strict same site enforcement.
*   `'lax'` will set the `SameSite` attribute to `Lax` for lax same site enforcement.
*   `'none'` will set the `SameSite` attribute to `None` for an explicit cross-site cookie.
*   `'strict'` will set the `SameSite` attribute to `Strict` for strict same site enforcement.

More information about enforcement levels can be found in [the specification](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-ietf-httpbis-rfc6265bis-09#section-5.4.7)
.

### `Optional`secure[](#secure)

secure?: boolean

Enables the [`Secure` `Set-Cookie` attribute](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-5.2.5)
. When enabled, clients will only send the cookie back if the browser has a HTTPS connection.

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

# Cookie | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [Cookie](react_router.Cookie.html)
    

Interface Cookie
================

A HTTP cookie.

A Cookie is a logical container for metadata about a HTTP cookie; its name and options. But it doesn't contain a value. Instead, it has `parse()` and `serialize()` methods that allow a single instance to be reused for parsing/encoding multiple different values.

#### See[](#See)

[https://remix.run/utils/cookies#cookie-api](https://remix.run/utils/cookies#cookie-api)

interface Cookie {  
    [expires](react_router.Cookie.html#expires)
?: Date;  
    [isSigned](react_router.Cookie.html#isSigned)
: boolean;  
    [name](react_router.Cookie.html#name)
: string;  
    [parse](react_router.Cookie.html#parse.parse-1)
(cookieHeader: null | string, options?: [CookieParseOptions](react_router.CookieParseOptions.html)
): Promise<any\>;  
    [serialize](react_router.Cookie.html#serialize.serialize-1)
(value: any, options?: [CookieSerializeOptions](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html)
): Promise<string\>;  
}

##### Index

### Properties

[expires?](react_router.Cookie.html#expires)
 [isSigned](react_router.Cookie.html#isSigned)
 [name](react_router.Cookie.html#name)

### Methods

[parse](react_router.Cookie.html#parse)
 [serialize](react_router.Cookie.html#serialize)

Properties
----------

### `Optional` `Readonly`expires[](#expires)

expires?: Date

The Date this cookie expires.

Note: This is calculated at access time using `maxAge` when no `expires` option is provided to `createCookie()`.

### `Readonly`isSigned[](#isSigned)

isSigned: boolean

True if this cookie uses one or more secrets for verification.

### `Readonly`name[](#name)

name: string

The name of the cookie, used in the `Cookie` and `Set-Cookie` headers.

Methods
-------

### parse[](#parse)

*   parse(cookieHeader, options?): Promise<any\>[](#parse.parse-1)
    
*   Parses a raw `Cookie` header and returns the value of this cookie or `null` if it's not present.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   cookieHeader: null | string
    *   `Optional`options: [CookieParseOptions](react_router.CookieParseOptions.html)
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<any\>
    

### serialize[](#serialize)

*   serialize(value, options?): Promise<string\>[](#serialize.serialize-1)
    
*   Serializes the given value to a string and returns the `Set-Cookie` header.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   value: any
    *   `Optional`options: [CookieSerializeOptions](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html)
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<string\>
    

### Settings

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

# CookieSignatureOptions | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [CookieSignatureOptions](react_router.CookieSignatureOptions.html)
    

Interface CookieSignatureOptions
================================

interface CookieSignatureOptions {  
    [secrets](react_router.CookieSignatureOptions.html#secrets)
?: string\[\];  
}

##### Index

### Properties

[secrets?](react_router.CookieSignatureOptions.html#secrets)

Properties
----------

### `Optional`secrets[](#secrets)

secrets?: string\[\]

An array of secrets that may be used to sign/unsign the value of a cookie.

The array makes it easy to rotate secrets. New secrets should be added to the beginning of the array. `cookie.serialize()` will always use the first value in the array, but `cookie.parse()` may use any of them so that cookies that were signed with older secrets still work.

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

# CookieParseOptions | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [CookieParseOptions](react_router.CookieParseOptions.html)
    

Interface CookieParseOptions
============================

Parse options.

interface CookieParseOptions {  
    [decode](react_router.CookieParseOptions.html#decode)
?: ((str: string) => undefined | string);  
}

##### Index

### Properties

[decode?](react_router.CookieParseOptions.html#decode)

Properties
----------

### `Optional`decode[](#decode)

decode?: ((str: string) => undefined | string)

Specifies a function that will be used to decode a [cookie-value](https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc6265#section-4.1.1)
. Since the value of a cookie has a limited character set (and must be a simple string), this function can be used to decode a previously-encoded cookie value into a JavaScript string.

The default function is the global `decodeURIComponent`, wrapped in a `try..catch`. If an error is thrown it will return the cookie's original value. If you provide your own encode/decode scheme you must ensure errors are appropriately handled.

#### Default[](#Default)

    decode
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

### On This Page

Properties

[decode](#decode)

preventScrollReset?: boolean

### `Optional`relative[](#relative)

relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)

Determines whether the form action is relative to the route hierarchy or the pathname. Use this if you want to opt out of navigating the route hierarchy and want to instead route based on /-delimited URL segments

# FetcherSubmitFunction | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [FetcherSubmitFunction](react_router.FetcherSubmitFunction.html)
    

Interface FetcherSubmitFunction
===============================

Submits a fetcher `<form>` to the server without reloading the page.

*   FetcherSubmitFunction(target, options?): Promise<void\>[](#FetcherSubmitFunction)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   target: [SubmitTarget](../types/react_router.SubmitTarget.html)
        
        Can be multiple types of elements and objects
        
        **`HTMLFormElement`**
        
            <fetcher.Form  onSubmit={(event) => {    fetcher.submit(event.currentTarget);  }}/>
            
        
        **`FormData`**
        
            const formData = new FormData();formData.append("myKey", "myValue");fetcher.submit(formData, { method: "post" });
            
        
        **Plain object that will be serialized as `FormData`**
        
            fetcher.submit({ myKey: "myValue" }, { method: "post" });
            
        
        **Plain object that will be serialized as JSON**
        
            fetcher.submit(  { myKey: "myValue" },  { method: "post", encType: "application/json" });
            
        
    *   `Optional`options: [FetcherSubmitOptions](react_router.FetcherSubmitOptions.html)
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

Properties
----------

### `Optional`about[](#about)

about?: string

### `Optional`acceptCharset[](#acceptCharset)

acceptCharset?: string

### `Optional`accessKey[](#accessKey)

accessKey?: string

### `Optional`action[](#action)

action?: string

The URL to submit the form data to. If `undefined`, this defaults to the closest route in context.

### `Optional`aria-activedescendant[](#aria_activedescendant)

aria-activedescendant?: string

Identifies the currently active element when DOM focus is on a composite widget, textbox, group, or application.

### `Optional`aria-atomic[](#aria_atomic)

aria-atomic?: Booleanish

Indicates whether assistive technologies will present all, or only parts of, the changed region based on the change notifications defined by the aria-relevant attribute.

### `Optional`aria-autocomplete[](#aria_autocomplete)

aria-autocomplete?:  
    | "none"  
    | "list"  
    | "inline"  
    | "both"

Indicates whether inputting text could trigger display of one or more predictions of the user's intended value for an input and specifies how predictions would be presented if they are made.

### `Optional`aria-braillelabel[](#aria_braillelabel)

aria-braillelabel?: string

Defines a string value that labels the current element, which is intended to be converted into Braille.

#### See[](#See)

aria-label.

### `Optional`aria-brailleroledescription[](#aria_brailleroledescription)

aria-brailleroledescription?: string

Defines a human-readable, author-localized abbreviated description for the role of an element, which is intended to be converted into Braille.

#### See[](#See-1)

aria-roledescription.

### `Optional`aria-busy[](#aria_busy)

aria-busy?: Booleanish

### `Optional`aria-checked[](#aria_checked)

aria-checked?:  
    | boolean  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "mixed"

Indicates the current "checked" state of checkboxes, radio buttons, and other widgets.

#### See[](#See-2)

*   aria-pressed
*   aria-selected.

### `Optional`aria-colcount[](#aria_colcount)

aria-colcount?: number

Defines the total number of columns in a table, grid, or treegrid.

#### See[](#See-3)

aria-colindex.

### `Optional`aria-colindex[](#aria_colindex)

aria-colindex?: number

Defines an element's column index or position with respect to the total number of columns within a table, grid, or treegrid.

#### See[](#See-4)

*   aria-colcount
*   aria-colspan.

### `Optional`aria-colindextext[](#aria_colindextext)

aria-colindextext?: string

Defines a human readable text alternative of aria-colindex.

#### See[](#See-5)

aria-rowindextext.

### `Optional`aria-colspan[](#aria_colspan)

aria-colspan?: number

Defines the number of columns spanned by a cell or gridcell within a table, grid, or treegrid.

#### See[](#See-6)

*   aria-colindex
*   aria-rowspan.

### `Optional`aria-controls[](#aria_controls)

aria-controls?: string

Identifies the element (or elements) whose contents or presence are controlled by the current element.

#### See[](#See-7)

aria-owns.

### `Optional`aria-current[](#aria_current)

aria-current?:  
    | boolean  
    | "time"  
    | "true"  
    | "location"  
    | "page"  
    | "step"  
    | "false"  
    | "date"

Indicates the element that represents the current item within a container or set of related elements.

### `Optional`aria-describedby[](#aria_describedby)

aria-describedby?: string

Identifies the element (or elements) that describes the object.

#### See[](#See-8)

aria-labelledby

### `Optional`aria-description[](#aria_description)

aria-description?: string

Defines a string value that describes or annotates the current element.

#### See[](#See-9)

related aria-describedby.

### `Optional`aria-details[](#aria_details)

aria-details?: string

Identifies the element that provides a detailed, extended description for the object.

#### See[](#See-10)

aria-describedby.

### `Optional`aria-disabled[](#aria_disabled)

aria-disabled?: Booleanish

Indicates that the element is perceivable but disabled, so it is not editable or otherwise operable.

#### See[](#See-11)

*   aria-hidden
*   aria-readonly.

### `Optional`aria-dropeffect[](#aria_dropeffect)

aria-dropeffect?:  
    | "link"  
    | "copy"  
    | "none"  
    | "execute"  
    | "move"  
    | "popup"

Indicates what functions can be performed when a dragged object is released on the drop target.

#### Deprecated[](#Deprecated)

in ARIA 1.1

### `Optional`aria-errormessage[](#aria_errormessage)

aria-errormessage?: string

Identifies the element that provides an error message for the object.

#### See[](#See-12)

*   aria-invalid
*   aria-describedby.

### `Optional`aria-expanded[](#aria_expanded)

aria-expanded?: Booleanish

Indicates whether the element, or another grouping element it controls, is currently expanded or collapsed.

### `Optional`aria-flowto[](#aria_flowto)

aria-flowto?: string

Identifies the next element (or elements) in an alternate reading order of content which, at the user's discretion, allows assistive technology to override the general default of reading in document source order.

### `Optional`aria-grabbed[](#aria_grabbed)

aria-grabbed?: Booleanish

Indicates an element's "grabbed" state in a drag-and-drop operation.

#### Deprecated[](#Deprecated-1)

in ARIA 1.1

### `Optional`aria-haspopup[](#aria_haspopup)

aria-haspopup?:  
    | boolean  
    | "dialog"  
    | "menu"  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "grid"  
    | "listbox"  
    | "tree"

Indicates the availability and type of interactive popup element, such as menu or dialog, that can be triggered by an element.

### `Optional`aria-hidden[](#aria_hidden)

aria-hidden?: Booleanish

Indicates whether the element is exposed to an accessibility API.

#### See[](#See-13)

aria-disabled.

### `Optional`aria-invalid[](#aria_invalid)

aria-invalid?:  
    | boolean  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "grammar"  
    | "spelling"

Indicates the entered value does not conform to the format expected by the application.

#### See[](#See-14)

aria-errormessage.

### `Optional`aria-keyshortcuts[](#aria_keyshortcuts)

aria-keyshortcuts?: string

Indicates keyboard shortcuts that an author has implemented to activate or give focus to an element.

### `Optional`aria-label[](#aria_label)

aria-label?: string

Defines a string value that labels the current element.

#### See[](#See-15)

aria-labelledby.

### `Optional`aria-labelledby[](#aria_labelledby)

aria-labelledby?: string

Identifies the element (or elements) that labels the current element.

#### See[](#See-16)

aria-describedby.

### `Optional`aria-level[](#aria_level)

aria-level?: number

Defines the hierarchical level of an element within a structure.

### `Optional`aria-live[](#aria_live)

aria-live?: "off" | "assertive" | "polite"

Indicates that an element will be updated, and describes the types of updates the user agents, assistive technologies, and user can expect from the live region.

### `Optional`aria-modal[](#aria_modal)

aria-modal?: Booleanish

Indicates whether an element is modal when displayed.

### `Optional`aria-multiline[](#aria_multiline)

aria-multiline?: Booleanish

Indicates whether a text box accepts multiple lines of input or only a single line.

### `Optional`aria-multiselectable[](#aria_multiselectable)

aria-multiselectable?: Booleanish

Indicates that the user may select more than one item from the current selectable descendants.

### `Optional`aria-orientation[](#aria_orientation)

aria-orientation?: "horizontal" | "vertical"

Indicates whether the element's orientation is horizontal, vertical, or unknown/ambiguous.

### `Optional`aria-owns[](#aria_owns)

aria-owns?: string

Identifies an element (or elements) in order to define a visual, functional, or contextual parent/child relationship between DOM elements where the DOM hierarchy cannot be used to represent the relationship.

#### See[](#See-17)

aria-controls.

### `Optional`aria-placeholder[](#aria_placeholder)

aria-placeholder?: string

Defines a short hint (a word or short phrase) intended to aid the user with data entry when the control has no value. A hint could be a sample value or a brief description of the expected format.

### `Optional`aria-posinset[](#aria_posinset)

aria-posinset?: number

Defines an element's number or position in the current set of listitems or treeitems. Not required if all elements in the set are present in the DOM.

#### See[](#See-18)

aria-setsize.

### `Optional`aria-pressed[](#aria_pressed)

aria-pressed?:  
    | boolean  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "mixed"

Indicates the current "pressed" state of toggle buttons.

#### See[](#See-19)

*   aria-checked
*   aria-selected.

### `Optional`aria-readonly[](#aria_readonly)

aria-readonly?: Booleanish

Indicates that the element is not editable, but is otherwise operable.

#### See[](#See-20)

aria-disabled.

### `Optional`aria-relevant[](#aria_relevant)

aria-relevant?:  
    | "text"  
    | "additions"  
    | "additions removals"  
    | "additions text"  
    | "all"  
    | "removals"  
    | "removals additions"  
    | "removals text"  
    | "text additions"  
    | "text removals"

Indicates what notifications the user agent will trigger when the accessibility tree within a live region is modified.

#### See[](#See-21)

aria-atomic.

### `Optional`aria-required[](#aria_required)

aria-required?: Booleanish

Indicates that user input is required on the element before a form may be submitted.

### `Optional`aria-roledescription[](#aria_roledescription)

aria-roledescription?: string

Defines a human-readable, author-localized description for the role of an element.

### `Optional`aria-rowcount[](#aria_rowcount)

Native `<form>` only supports `get` and `post`, avoid the other verbs if you'd like to support progressive enhancement

# HeadersFunction | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [HeadersFunction](react_router.HeadersFunction.html)
    

Interface HeadersFunction
=========================

A function that returns HTTP headers to be used for a route. These headers will be merged with (and take precedence over) headers from parent routes.

*   HeadersFunction(args): HeadersInit[](#HeadersFunction)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   args: [HeadersArgs](../types/react_router.HeadersArgs.html)
        
    
    #### Returns HeadersInit
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# HashRouterProps | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [HashRouterProps](react_router.HashRouterProps.html)
    

Interface HashRouterProps
=========================

interface HashRouterProps {  
    [basename](react_router.HashRouterProps.html#basename)
?: string;  
    [children](react_router.HashRouterProps.html#children)
?: ReactNode;  
    [window](react_router.HashRouterProps.html#window)
?: Window;  
}

The URL to submit the form data to. If `undefined`, this defaults to the closest route in context.

### `Optional`aria-activedescendant[](#aria_activedescendant)

aria-activedescendant?: string

Identifies the currently active element when DOM focus is on a composite widget, textbox, group, or application.

### `Optional`aria-atomic[](#aria_atomic)

aria-atomic?: Booleanish

Indicates whether assistive technologies will present all, or only parts of, the changed region based on the change notifications defined by the aria-relevant attribute.

### `Optional`aria-autocomplete[](#aria_autocomplete)

aria-autocomplete?:  
    | "none"  
    | "list"  
    | "inline"  
    | "both"

Indicates whether inputting text could trigger display of one or more predictions of the user's intended value for an input and specifies how predictions would be presented if they are made.

### `Optional`aria-braillelabel[](#aria_braillelabel)

aria-braillelabel?: string

Defines a string value that labels the current element, which is intended to be converted into Braille.

#### See[](#See)

aria-label.

### `Optional`aria-brailleroledescription[](#aria_brailleroledescription)

aria-brailleroledescription?: string

Defines a human-readable, author-localized abbreviated description for the role of an element, which is intended to be converted into Braille.

#### See[](#See-1)

aria-roledescription.

### `Optional`aria-busy[](#aria_busy)

    | boolean  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "mixed"

*   aria-pressed
*   aria-selected.

    | "step"  
    | "false"  
    | "date"

### `Optional`aria-flowto[](#aria_flowto)

### `Optional`relative[](#relative)

relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)

Determines whether the form action is relative to the route hierarchy or the pathname. Use this if you want to opt out of navigating the route hierarchy and want to instead route based on /-delimited URL segments

### `Optional`reloadDocument[](#reloadDocument)

reloadDocument?: boolean

Forces a full document navigation instead of client side routing + data fetch.

### `Optional`replace[](#replace)

replace?: boolean

Replaces the current entry in the browser history stack when the form navigates. Use this if you don't want the user to be able to click "back" to the page with the form on it.

?: ReactNode;

# Location | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)

Interface Location<State>
=========================

An entry in a history stack. A location contains information about the URL path, as well as possibly some arbitrary state and a key.

interface Location<[State](react_router.Location.html#State)
\> {  
    [hash](react_router.Location.html#hash)
: string;  
    [key](react_router.Location.html#key)
: string;  
    [pathname](react_router.Location.html#pathname)
: string;  
    [search](react_router.Location.html#search)
: string;  
    [state](react_router.Location.html#state-1)
: [State](react_router.Location.html#State)
;  
}

#### Type Parameters

*   State = any

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#react-router.Location)
)

*   [Path](react_router.Path.html)
    *   Location

##### Index

### Properties

[hash](react_router.Location.html#hash)
 [key](react_router.Location.html#key)
 [pathname](react_router.Location.html#pathname)
 [search](react_router.Location.html#search)
 [state](react_router.Location.html#state-1)

Properties
----------

### hash[](#hash)

hash: string

A URL fragment identifier, beginning with a #.

### key[](#key)

key: string

A unique string associated with this location. May be used to safely store and retrieve data in some other storage API, like `localStorage`.

Note: This value is always "default" on the initial location.

### pathname[](#pathname)

pathname: string

A URL pathname, beginning with a /.

### search[](#search)

search: string

A URL search string, beginning with a ?.

### state[](#state-1)

state: [State](react_router.Location.html#State)

A value of arbitrary data associated with this location.

# MetaFunction | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [MetaFunction](react_router.MetaFunction.html)
    

Interface MetaFunction<Loader, MatchLoaders>
============================================

A function that returns an array of data objects to use for rendering metadata HTML tags in a route. These tags are not rendered on descendant routes in the route hierarchy. In other words, they will only be rendered on the route in which they are exported.

#### Type Parameters

*   Loader extends [LoaderFunction](../types/react_router.LoaderFunction.html)
     | [ClientLoaderFunction](../types/react_router.ClientLoaderFunction.html)
     | unknown = unknown
    
    The type of the current route's loader function
    
*   MatchLoaders extends Record<string, [LoaderFunction](../types/react_router.LoaderFunction.html)
     | [ClientLoaderFunction](../types/react_router.ClientLoaderFunction.html)
     | unknown\> = Record<string, unknown\>
    
    Mapping from a parent route's filepath to its loader function type
    
    Note that parent route filepaths are relative to the `app/` directory.
    
    For example, if this meta function is for `/sales/customers/$customerId`:
    
        // app/root.tsxconst loader = () => ({ hello: "world" })export type Loader = typeof loader// app/routes/sales.tsxconst loader = () => ({ salesCount: 1074 })export type Loader = typeof loader// app/routes/sales/customers.tsxconst loader = () => ({ customerCount: 74 })export type Loader = typeof loader// app/routes/sales/customers/$customersId.tsximport type { Loader as RootLoader } from "../../../root"import type { Loader as SalesLoader } from "../../sales"import type { Loader as CustomersLoader } from "../../sales/customers"const loader = () => ({ name: "Customer name" })const meta: MetaFunction<typeof loader, { "root": RootLoader, "routes/sales": SalesLoader, "routes/sales/customers": CustomersLoader,}> = ({ data, matches }) => {  const { name } = data  //      ^? string  const { customerCount } = matches.find((match) => match.id === "routes/sales/customers").data  //      ^? number  const { salesCount } = matches.find((match) => match.id === "routes/sales").data  //      ^? number  const { hello } = matches.find((match) => match.id === "root").data  //      ^? "world"}
        
    

*   MetaFunction(args): undefined | [MetaDescriptor](../types/react_router.MetaDescriptor.html)
    \[\][](#MetaFunction)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   args: [MetaArgs](react_router.MetaArgs.html)
        <[Loader](react_router.MetaFunction.html#Loader)
        , [MatchLoaders](react_router.MetaFunction.html#MatchLoaders)
        \>
    
    #### Returns undefined | [MetaDescriptor](../types/react_router.MetaDescriptor.html)
    \[\]
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

=====================

    [context](react_router.OutletProps.html#context)
?: unknown;

##### Index

### Properties

[context?](react_router.OutletProps.html#context)

Properties
----------

### `Optional`context[](#context)

context?: unknown

Provides a context value to the element tree below the outlet. Use when the parent route needs to provide values to child routes.

    <Outlet context={myContextValue} />
    

Access the context with [useOutletContext](../functions/react_router.useOutletContext.html)
.

*   Inherited

# PathMatch | React Router API Reference

Interface PathMatch<ParamKey>
=============================

A PathMatch contains info about how a PathPattern matched on a URL pathname.

interface PathMatch<[ParamKey](react_router.PathMatch.html#ParamKey)
\> {  
    [params](react_router.PathMatch.html#params)
: [Params](../types/react_router.Params.html)
<[ParamKey](react_router.PathMatch.html#ParamKey)
\>;  
    [pathname](react_router.PathMatch.html#pathname)
: string;  
    [pathnameBase](react_router.PathMatch.html#pathnameBase)
: string;  
    [pattern](react_router.PathMatch.html#pattern)
: [PathPattern](react_router.PathPattern.html)
<string\>;  
}

#### Type Parameters

*   ParamKey extends string = string

##### Index

### Properties

[params](react_router.PathMatch.html#params)
 [pathname](react_router.PathMatch.html#pathname)
 [pathnameBase](react_router.PathMatch.html#pathnameBase)
 [pattern](react_router.PathMatch.html#pattern)

Properties
----------

### params[](#params)

params: [Params](../types/react_router.Params.html)
<[ParamKey](react_router.PathMatch.html#ParamKey)
\>

The names and values of dynamic parameters in the URL.

### pathname[](#pathname)

pathname: string

The portion of the URL pathname that was matched.

### pathnameBase[](#pathnameBase)

pathnameBase: string

The portion of the URL pathname that was matched before child routes.

### pattern[](#pattern)

pattern: [PathPattern](react_router.PathPattern.html)
<string\>

The pattern that was used to match.

Properties
----------

### `Optional`about[](#about)

about?: string

### `Optional`accessKey[](#accessKey)

accessKey?: string

### `Optional`aria-activedescendant[](#aria_activedescendant)

aria-activedescendant?: string

Identifies the currently active element when DOM focus is on a composite widget, textbox, group, or application.

### `Optional`aria-atomic[](#aria_atomic)

aria-atomic?: Booleanish

Indicates whether assistive technologies will present all, or only parts of, the changed region based on the change notifications defined by the aria-relevant attribute.

### `Optional`aria-autocomplete[](#aria_autocomplete)

aria-autocomplete?:  
    | "none"  
    | "list"  
    | "inline"  
    | "both"

Indicates whether inputting text could trigger display of one or more predictions of the user's intended value for an input and specifies how predictions would be presented if they are made.

### `Optional`aria-braillelabel[](#aria_braillelabel)

aria-braillelabel?: string

Defines a string value that labels the current element, which is intended to be converted into Braille.

#### See[](#See)

aria-label.

### `Optional`aria-brailleroledescription[](#aria_brailleroledescription)

aria-brailleroledescription?: string

Defines a human-readable, author-localized abbreviated description for the role of an element, which is intended to be converted into Braille.

#### See[](#See-1)

aria-roledescription.

### `Optional`aria-busy[](#aria_busy)

aria-busy?: Booleanish

### `Optional`aria-checked[](#aria_checked)

aria-checked?:  
    | boolean  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "mixed"

Indicates the current "checked" state of checkboxes, radio buttons, and other widgets.

#### See[](#See-2)

*   aria-pressed
*   aria-selected.

### `Optional`aria-colcount[](#aria_colcount)

aria-colcount?: number

Defines the total number of columns in a table, grid, or treegrid.

#### See[](#See-3)

aria-colindex.

### `Optional`aria-colindex[](#aria_colindex)

aria-colindex?: number

Defines an element's column index or position with respect to the total number of columns within a table, grid, or treegrid.

#### See[](#See-4)

*   aria-colcount
*   aria-colspan.

### `Optional`aria-colindextext[](#aria_colindextext)

aria-colindextext?: string

Defines a human readable text alternative of aria-colindex.

#### See[](#See-5)

aria-rowindextext.

### `Optional`aria-colspan[](#aria_colspan)

aria-colspan?: number

Defines the number of columns spanned by a cell or gridcell within a table, grid, or treegrid.

#### See[](#See-6)

*   aria-colindex
*   aria-rowspan.

### `Optional`aria-controls[](#aria_controls)

aria-controls?: string

Identifies the element (or elements) whose contents or presence are controlled by the current element.

#### See[](#See-7)

aria-owns.

### `Optional`aria-current[](#aria_current)

aria-current?:  
    | boolean  
    | "time"  
    | "true"  
    | "location"  
    | "page"  
    | "step"  
    | "false"  
    | "date"

Indicates the element that represents the current item within a container or set of related elements.

### `Optional`aria-describedby[](#aria_describedby)

aria-describedby?: string

Identifies the element (or elements) that describes the object.

#### See[](#See-8)

aria-labelledby

### `Optional`aria-description[](#aria_description)

aria-description?: string

Defines a string value that describes or annotates the current element.

#### See[](#See-9)

related aria-describedby.

### `Optional`aria-details[](#aria_details)

aria-details?: string

Identifies the element that provides a detailed, extended description for the object.

#### See[](#See-10)

aria-describedby.

### `Optional`aria-disabled[](#aria_disabled)

aria-disabled?: Booleanish

Indicates that the element is perceivable but disabled, so it is not editable or otherwise operable.

#### See[](#See-11)

*   aria-hidden
*   aria-readonly.

### `Optional`aria-dropeffect[](#aria_dropeffect)

aria-dropeffect?:  
    | "link"  
    | "copy"  
    | "none"  
    | "execute"  
    | "move"  
    | "popup"

Indicates what functions can be performed when a dragged object is released on the drop target.

#### Deprecated[](#Deprecated)

in ARIA 1.1

### `Optional`aria-errormessage[](#aria_errormessage)

aria-errormessage?: string

Identifies the element that provides an error message for the object.

#### See[](#See-12)

*   aria-invalid
*   aria-describedby.

### `Optional`aria-expanded[](#aria_expanded)

aria-expanded?: Booleanish

Indicates whether the element, or another grouping element it controls, is currently expanded or collapsed.

### `Optional`aria-flowto[](#aria_flowto)

aria-flowto?: string

Identifies the next element (or elements) in an alternate reading order of content which, at the user's discretion, allows assistive technology to override the general default of reading in document source order.

### `Optional`aria-grabbed[](#aria_grabbed)

aria-grabbed?: Booleanish

Indicates an element's "grabbed" state in a drag-and-drop operation.

#### Deprecated[](#Deprecated-1)

in ARIA 1.1

### `Optional`aria-haspopup[](#aria_haspopup)

aria-haspopup?:  
    | boolean  
    | "dialog"  
    | "menu"  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "grid"  
    | "listbox"  
    | "tree"

Indicates the availability and type of interactive popup element, such as menu or dialog, that can be triggered by an element.

aria-hidden?: Booleanish

aria-disabled.

aria-invalid?:  
    | boolean  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "grammar"  
    | "spelling"

Indicates the entered value does not conform to the format expected by the application.

aria-errormessage.

### `Optional`aria-keyshortcuts[](#aria_keyshortcuts)

aria-keyshortcuts?: string

Indicates keyboard shortcuts that an author has implemented to activate or give focus to an element.

aria-label?: string

Defines a string value that labels the current element.

#### See[](#See-15)

aria-labelledby?: string

Identifies the element (or elements) that labels the current element.

#### See[](#See-16)

aria-describedby.

### `Optional`aria-level[](#aria_level)

aria-level?: number

Defines the hierarchical level of an element within a structure.

### `Optional`aria-live[](#aria_live)

aria-live?: "off" | "assertive" | "polite"

Indicates that an element will be updated, and describes the types of updates the user agents, assistive technologies, and user can expect from the live region.

### `Optional`aria-modal[](#aria_modal)

aria-modal?: Booleanish

Indicates whether an element is modal when displayed.

### `Optional`aria-multiline[](#aria_multiline)

aria-multiline?: Booleanish

Indicates whether a text box accepts multiple lines of input or only a single line.

### `Optional`aria-multiselectable[](#aria_multiselectable)

aria-multiselectable?: Booleanish

Indicates that the user may select more than one item from the current selectable descendants.

### `Optional`aria-orientation[](#aria_orientation)

aria-orientation?: "horizontal" | "vertical"

Indicates whether the element's orientation is horizontal, vertical, or unknown/ambiguous.

### `Optional`aria-owns[](#aria_owns)

aria-owns?: string

Identifies an element (or elements) in order to define a visual, functional, or contextual parent/child relationship between DOM elements where the DOM hierarchy cannot be used to represent the relationship.

#### See[](#See-17)

aria-controls.

### `Optional`aria-placeholder[](#aria_placeholder)

aria-placeholder?: string

Defines a short hint (a word or short phrase) intended to aid the user with data entry when the control has no value. A hint could be a sample value or a brief description of the expected format.

### `Optional`aria-posinset[](#aria_posinset)

aria-posinset?: number

Defines an element's number or position in the current set of listitems or treeitems. Not required if all elements in the set are present in the DOM.

#### See[](#See-18)

aria-setsize.

### `Optional`aria-pressed[](#aria_pressed)

    | boolean  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "mixed"

Indicates the current "pressed" state of toggle buttons.

*   aria-checked
*   aria-selected.

### `Optional`aria-readonly[](#aria_readonly)

aria-readonly?: Booleanish

Indicates that the element is not editable, but is otherwise operable.

#### See[](#See-20)

aria-disabled.

### `Optional`aria-relevant[](#aria_relevant)

aria-relevant?:  
    | "text"  
    | "additions"  
    | "additions removals"  
    | "additions text"  
    | "all"  
    | "removals"  
    | "removals additions"  
    | "removals text"  
    | "text additions"  
    | "text removals"

Indicates what notifications the user agent will trigger when the accessibility tree within a live region is modified.

#### See[](#See-21)

aria-atomic.

### `Optional`discover[](#discover)

discover?: DiscoverBehavior

Defines the link discovery behavior

    <Link /> // default ("render")<Link discover="render" /><Link discover="none" />
    

*   **render** - default, discover the route when the link renders
*   **none** - don't eagerly discover, only discover if the link is clicked

### `Optional`ping[](#ping)

ping?: string

### `Optional`placeholder[](#placeholder)

placeholder?: string

### `Optional`prefetch[](#prefetch)

prefetch?: PrefetchBehavior

Defines the data and module prefetching behavior for the link.

    <Link /> // default<Link prefetch="none" /><Link prefetch="intent" /><Link prefetch="render" /><Link prefetch="viewport" />
    

*   **none** - default, no prefetching
*   **intent** - prefetches when the user hovers or focuses the link
*   **render** - prefetches when the link renders
*   **viewport** - prefetches when the link is in the viewport, very useful for mobile

Prefetching is done with HTML `<link rel="prefetch">` tags. They are inserted after the link.

    <a href="..." /><a href="..." /><link rel="prefetch" /> // might conditionally render
    

Because of this, if you are using `nav :last-child` you will need to use `nav :last-of-type` so the styles don't conditionally fall off your last link (and any other similar selectors).

### `Optional`prefix[](#prefix)

prefix?: string

### `Optional`preventScrollReset[](#preventScrollReset)

preventScrollReset?: boolean

Prevents the scroll position from being reset to the top of the window when the link is clicked and the app is using [ScrollRestoration](../functions/react_router.ScrollRestoration.html)
. This only prevents new locations reseting scroll to the top, scroll position will be restored for back/forward button navigation.

    <Link to="?tab=one" preventScrollReset />
    

### `Optional`property[](#property)

property?: string

### `Optional`radioGroup[](#radioGroup)

radioGroup?: string

### `Optional`referrerPolicy[](#referrerPolicy)

referrerPolicy?: HTMLAttributeReferrerPolicy

### `Optional`rel[](#rel)

rel?: string

### `Optional`relative[](#relative)

relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)

Defines the relative path behavior for the link.

    <Link to=".." /> // default: "route"<Link relative="route" /><Link relative="path" />
    

Consider a route hierarchy where a parent route pattern is "blog" and a child route pattern is "blog/:slug/edit".

*   **route** - default, resolves the link relative to the route pattern. In the example above a relative link of `".."` will remove both `:slug/edit` segments back to "/blog".
*   **path** - relative to the path so `..` will only remove one URL segment up to "/blog/:slug"

### `Optional`reloadDocument[](#reloadDocument)

reloadDocument?: boolean

Will use document navigation instead of client side routing when the link is clicked: the browser will handle the transition normally (as if it were an `<a href>`).

    <Link to="/logout" reloadDocument />
    

### `Optional`replace[](#replace)

replace?: boolean

Replaces the current entry in the history stack instead of pushing a new one onto it.

    <Link replace />
    

    # with a history stack like thisA -> B# normal link click pushes a new entryA -> B -> C# but with `replace`, B is replaced by CA -> C
    

### `Optional`resource[](#resource)

resource?: string

### `Optional`results[](#results)

results?: number

### `Optional`rev[](#rev)

rev?: string

### `Optional`role[](#role)

role?: AriaRole

### `Optional`security[](#security)

security?: string

### `Optional`slot[](#slot)

slot?: string

### `Optional`spellCheck[](#spellCheck)

spellCheck?: Booleanish

### `Optional`state[](#state)

state?: any

Adds persistent client side routing state to the next location.

    <Link to="/somewhere/else" state={{ some: "value" }} />
    

The location state is accessed from the `location`.

    function SomeComp() {  const location = useLocation()  location.state; // { some: "value" }}
    

This state is inaccessible on the server as it is implemented on top of [`history.state`](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/History/state)

### `Optional`style[](#style)

style?: CSSProperties

### `Optional`tabIndex[](#tabIndex)

### `Optional`target[](#target)

target?: HTMLAttributeAnchorTarget

### `Optional`title[](#title)

title?: string

### to[](#to)

to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)

Can be a string or a partial [Path](react_router.Path.html)
:

    <Link to="/some/path" /><Link  to={{    pathname: "/some/path",    search: "?query=string",    hash: "#hash",  }}/>

### `Optional`viewTransition[](#viewTransition)

viewTransition?: boolean

Enables a [View Transition](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/View_Transitions_API)
 for this navigation.

    
      Click me
    
    

To apply specific styles for the transition, see [useViewTransitionState](../functions/react_router.useViewTransitionState.html)

### `Optional`vocab[](#vocab)

vocab?: string

# Navigator | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [Navigator](react_router.Navigator.html)
    

Interface Navigator
===================

A Navigator is a "location changer"; it's how you get to different locations.

Every history instance conforms to the Navigator interface, but the distinction is useful primarily when it comes to the low-level `<Router>` API where both the location and a navigator must be provided separately in order to avoid "tearing" that may occur in a suspense-enabled app if the action and/or location were to be read directly from the history instance.

interface Navigator {  
    [createHref](react_router.Navigator.html#createHref)
: ((to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
) => string);  
    [encodeLocation](react_router.Navigator.html#encodeLocation)
?: ((to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
) => [Path](react_router.Path.html)
);  
    [go](react_router.Navigator.html#go)
: ((delta: number) => void);  
    [push](react_router.Navigator.html#push.push-1)
(to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
, state?: any, opts?: [NavigateOptions](react_router.NavigateOptions.html)
): void;  
    [replace](react_router.Navigator.html#replace.replace-1)
(to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
, state?: any, opts?: [NavigateOptions](react_router.NavigateOptions.html)
): void;  
}

##### Index

### Properties

[createHref](react_router.Navigator.html#createHref)
 [encodeLocation?](react_router.Navigator.html#encodeLocation)
 [go](react_router.Navigator.html#go)

### Methods

[push](react_router.Navigator.html#push)
 [replace](react_router.Navigator.html#replace)

Properties
----------

### createHref[](#createHref)

createHref: ((to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
) => string)

#### Type declaration

*   *   (to): string
    *   Returns a valid href for the given `to` value that may be used as the value of an attribute.
        
        #### Parameters
        
        *   to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
            
            The destination URL
            
        
        #### Returns string
        

### `Optional`encodeLocation[](#encodeLocation)

encodeLocation?: ((to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
) => [Path](react_router.Path.html)
)

#### Type declaration

*   *   (to): [Path](react_router.Path.html)
        
    *   Encode a location the same way window.history would do (no-op for memory history) so we ensure our PUSH/REPLACE navigations for data routers behave the same as POP
        
        #### Parameters
        
        *   to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
            
            Unencoded path
            
        
        #### Returns [Path](react_router.Path.html)
        

### go[](#go)

go: ((delta: number) => void)

#### Type declaration

*   *   (delta): void
    *   Navigates `n` entries backward/forward in the history stack relative to the current index. For example, a "back" navigation would use go(-1).
        
        #### Parameters
        
        *   delta: number
            
            The delta in the stack index
            
        
        #### Returns void
        

Methods
-------

### push[](#push)

*   push(to, state?, opts?): void[](#push.push-1)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
        
    *   `Optional`state: any
    *   `Optional`opts: [NavigateOptions](react_router.NavigateOptions.html)
        
    
    #### Returns void
    

### replace[](#replace)

*   replace(to, state?, opts?): void[](#replace.replace-1)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
        
    *   `Optional`state: any
    *   `Optional`opts: [NavigateOptions](react_router.NavigateOptions.html)
        
    
    #### Returns void

about?: string

### `Optional`accessKey[](#accessKey)

accessKey?: string

### `Optional`aria-activedescendant[](#aria_activedescendant)

aria-activedescendant?: string

Identifies the currently active element when DOM focus is on a composite widget, textbox, group, or application.

### `Optional`aria-atomic[](#aria_atomic)

aria-atomic?: Booleanish

Indicates whether assistive technologies will present all, or only parts of, the changed region based on the change notifications defined by the aria-relevant attribute.

### `Optional`aria-autocomplete[](#aria_autocomplete)

aria-autocomplete?:  
    | "none"  
    | "list"  
    | "inline"  
    | "both"

Indicates whether inputting text could trigger display of one or more predictions of the user's intended value for an input and specifies how predictions would be presented if they are made.

### `Optional`aria-braillelabel[](#aria_braillelabel)

aria-braillelabel?: string

Defines a string value that labels the current element, which is intended to be converted into Braille.

#### See[](#See)

aria-label.

### `Optional`aria-brailleroledescription[](#aria_brailleroledescription)

aria-brailleroledescription?: string

Defines a human-readable, author-localized abbreviated description for the role of an element, which is intended to be converted into Braille.

#### See[](#See-1)

aria-roledescription.

### `Optional`aria-busy[](#aria_busy)

    | boolean  
    | "true"  
    | "false"  
    | "mixed"

#### See[](#See-2)

*   aria-pressed
*   aria-selected.

### `Optional`aria-colcount[](#aria_colcount)

aria-colcount?: number

#### See[](#See-3)

*   aria-colspan.

*   aria-rowspan.

aria-flowto?: string

Identifies the next element (or elements) in an alternate reading order of content which, at the user's discretion, allows assistive technology to override the general default of reading in document source order.

### `Optional`caseSensitive[](#caseSensitive)

caseSensitive?: boolean

Changes the matching logic to make it case-sensitive:

| Link | URL | isActive |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `<NavLink to="/SpOnGe-bOB" />` | `/sponge-bob` | true |
| `<NavLink to="/SpOnGe-bOB" caseSensitive />` | `/sponge-bob` | false |

### `Optional`children[](#children)

children?: ReactNode | ((props: [NavLinkRenderProps](../types/react_router.NavLinkRenderProps.html)
) => ReactNode)

Can be regular React children or a function that receives an object with the active and pending states of the link.

    <NavLink to="/tasks">  {({ isActive }) => (    <span className={isActive ? "active" : ""}>Tasks</span>  )}</NavLink>
    

### `Optional`className[](#className)

className?: string | ((props: [NavLinkRenderProps](../types/react_router.NavLinkRenderProps.html)
) => undefined | string)

Classes are automatically applied to NavLink that correspond to [NavLinkRenderProps](../types/react_router.NavLinkRenderProps.html)
.

    a.active { color: red; }a.pending { color: blue; }a.transitioning {  view-transition-name: my-transition;}

### `Optional`dir[](#dir)

dir?: string

### `Optional`discover[](#discover)

discover?: DiscoverBehavior

Defines the link discovery behavior

    <Link /> // default ("render")<Link discover="render" /><Link discover="none" />
    

*   **render** - default, discover the route when the link renders
*   **none** - don't eagerly discover, only discover if the link is clicked

### `Optional`download[](#download)

download?: any

### `Optional`draggable[](#draggable)

draggable?: Booleanish

### `Optional`end[](#end)

end?: boolean

Changes the matching logic for the `active` and `pending` states to only match to the "end" of the [NavLinkProps.to](react_router.NavLinkProps.html#to)
. If the URL is longer, it will no longer be considered active.

| Link | URL | isActive |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `<NavLink to="/tasks" />` | `/tasks` | true |
| `<NavLink to="/tasks" />` | `/tasks/123` | true |
| `<NavLink to="/tasks" end />` | `/tasks` | true |
| `<NavLink to="/tasks" end />` | `/tasks/123` | false |

`<NavLink to="/">` is an exceptional case because _every_ URL matches `/`. To avoid this matching every single route by default, it effectively ignores the `end` prop and only matches when you're at the root route.

### `Optional`ping[](#ping)

ping?: string

### `Optional`placeholder[](#placeholder)

placeholder?: string

### `Optional`prefetch[](#prefetch)

prefetch?: PrefetchBehavior

Defines the data and module prefetching behavior for the link.

    <Link /> // default<Link prefetch="none" /><Link prefetch="intent" /><Link prefetch="render" /><Link prefetch="viewport" />
    

*   **none** - default, no prefetching
*   **intent** - prefetches when the user hovers or focuses the link
*   **render** - prefetches when the link renders
*   **viewport** - prefetches when the link is in the viewport, very useful for mobile

Prefetching is done with HTML `<link rel="prefetch">` tags. They are inserted after the link.

    <a href="..." /><a href="..." /><link rel="prefetch" /> // might conditionally render
    

Because of this, if you are using `nav :last-child` you will need to use `nav :last-of-type` so the styles don't conditionally fall off your last link (and any other similar selectors).

### `Optional`prefix[](#prefix)

prefix?: string

### `Optional`preventScrollReset[](#preventScrollReset)

preventScrollReset?: boolean

Prevents the scroll position from being reset to the top of the window when the link is clicked and the app is using [ScrollRestoration](../functions/react_router.ScrollRestoration.html)
. This only prevents new locations reseting scroll to the top, scroll position will be restored for back/forward button navigation.

    <Link to="?tab=one" preventScrollReset />
    

### `Optional`property[](#property)

property?: string

### `Optional`radioGroup[](#radioGroup)

radioGroup?: string

### `Optional`referrerPolicy[](#referrerPolicy)

referrerPolicy?: HTMLAttributeReferrerPolicy

### `Optional`rel[](#rel)

rel?: string

### `Optional`relative[](#relative)

relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)

Defines the relative path behavior for the link.

    <Link to=".." /> // default: "route"<Link relative="route" /><Link relative="path" />
    

Consider a route hierarchy where a parent route pattern is "blog" and a child route pattern is "blog/:slug/edit".

*   **route** - default, resolves the link relative to the route pattern. In the example above a relative link of `".."` will remove both `:slug/edit` segments back to "/blog".
*   **path** - relative to the path so `..` will only remove one URL segment up to "/blog/:slug"

### `Optional`reloadDocument[](#reloadDocument)

reloadDocument?: boolean

Will use document navigation instead of client side routing when the link is clicked: the browser will handle the transition normally (as if it were an `<a href>`).

    <Link to="/logout" reloadDocument />
    

### `Optional`replace[](#replace)

replace?: boolean

Replaces the current entry in the history stack instead of pushing a new one onto it.

    <Link replace />
    

    # with a history stack like thisA -> B# normal link click pushes a new entryA -> B -> C# but with `replace`, B is replaced by CA -> C
    

### `Optional`resource[](#resource)

resource?: string

### `Optional`results[](#results)

results?: number

### `Optional`rev[](#rev)

rev?: string

### `Optional`role[](#role)

role?: AriaRole

### `Optional`security[](#security)

security?: string

### `Optional`slot[](#slot)

slot?: string

### `Optional`spellCheck[](#spellCheck)

spellCheck?: Booleanish

### `Optional`state[](#state)

state?: any

Adds persistent client side routing state to the next location.

    <Link to="/somewhere/else" state={{ some: "value" }} />
    

The location state is accessed from the `location`.

    function SomeComp() {  const location = useLocation()  location.state; // { some: "value" }}
    

This state is inaccessible on the server as it is implemented on top of [`history.state`](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/History/state)

### `Optional`style[](#style)

style?: CSSProperties | ((props: [NavLinkRenderProps](../types/react_router.NavLinkRenderProps.html)
) => undefined | CSSProperties)

### `Optional`tabIndex[](#tabIndex)

### `Optional`target[](#target)

target?: HTMLAttributeAnchorTarget

### `Optional`title[](#title)

title?: string

### to[](#to)

to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)

Can be a string or a partial [Path](react_router.Path.html)
:

    <Link to="/some/path" /><Link  to={{    pathname: "/some/path",    search: "?query=string",    hash: "#hash",  }}/>

### `Optional`viewTransition[](#viewTransition)

viewTransition?: boolean

Enables a [View Transition](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/View_Transitions_API)
 for this navigation.

    
      Click me
    
    

To apply specific styles for the transition, see [useViewTransitionState](../functions/react_router.useViewTransitionState.html)

# PathPattern | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [PathPattern](react_router.PathPattern.html)
    

Interface PathPattern<Path>
===========================

A PathPattern is used to match on some portion of a URL pathname.

interface PathPattern<[Path](react_router.PathPattern.html#Path)
\> {  
    [caseSensitive](react_router.PathPattern.html#caseSensitive)
?: boolean;  
    [end](react_router.PathPattern.html#end)
?: boolean;  
    [path](react_router.PathPattern.html#path-1)
: [Path](react_router.PathPattern.html#Path)
;  
}

#### Type Parameters

*   Path extends string = string

##### Index

### Properties

[caseSensitive?](react_router.PathPattern.html#caseSensitive)
 [end?](react_router.PathPattern.html#end)
 [path](react_router.PathPattern.html#path-1)

Properties
----------

### `Optional`caseSensitive[](#caseSensitive)

caseSensitive?: boolean

Should be `true` if the static portions of the `path` should be matched in the same case.

### `Optional`end[](#end)

end?: boolean

Should be `true` if this pattern should match the entire URL pathname.

### path[](#path-1)

path: [Path](react_router.PathPattern.html#Path)

A string to match against a URL pathname. May contain `:id`\-style segments to indicate placeholders for dynamic parameters. May also end with `/*` to indicate matching the rest of the URL pathname.

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

### On This Page

Properties

[caseSensitive](#caseSensitive)
[end](#end)
[path](#path-1)

---

# RouteMatch | React Router API Reference

Interface RouteMatch<ParamKey, RouteObjectType>
===============================================

interface RouteMatch<[ParamKey](react_router.RouteMatch.html#ParamKey)
, [RouteObjectType](react_router.RouteMatch.html#RouteObjectType)
\> {  
    [params](react_router.RouteMatch.html#params)
: [Params](../types/react_router.Params.html)
<[ParamKey](react_router.RouteMatch.html#ParamKey)
\>;  
    [pathname](react_router.RouteMatch.html#pathname)
: string;  
    [pathnameBase](react_router.RouteMatch.html#pathnameBase)
: string;  
    [route](react_router.RouteMatch.html#route)
: [RouteObjectType](react_router.RouteMatch.html#RouteObjectType)
;  
}

#### Type Parameters

*   ParamKey extends string = string
*   RouteObjectType extends [RouteObject](../types/react_router.RouteObject.html)
     = [RouteObject](../types/react_router.RouteObject.html)
    

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#react-router.RouteMatch)
)

*   AgnosticRouteMatch<[ParamKey](react_router.RouteMatch.html#ParamKey)
    , [RouteObjectType](react_router.RouteMatch.html#RouteObjectType)
    \>
    *   RouteMatch
        *   [DataRouteMatch](react_router.DataRouteMatch.html)
            

##### Index

### Properties

[params](react_router.RouteMatch.html#params)
 [pathname](react_router.RouteMatch.html#pathname)
 [pathnameBase](react_router.RouteMatch.html#pathnameBase)
 [route](react_router.RouteMatch.html#route)

Properties
----------

### params[](#params)

params: [Params](../types/react_router.Params.html)
<[ParamKey](react_router.RouteMatch.html#ParamKey)
\>

The names and values of dynamic parameters in the URL.

### pathname[](#pathname)

pathname: string

The portion of the URL pathname that was matched.

### pathnameBase[](#pathnameBase)

pathnameBase: string

The portion of the URL pathname that was matched before child routes.

### route[](#route)

route: [RouteObjectType](react_router.RouteMatch.html#RouteObjectType)

The route object that was used to match.

# RouterState | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [RouterState](react_router.RouterState.html)
    

Interface RouterState
=====================

State maintained internally by the router. During a navigation, all states reflect the the "old" location unless otherwise noted.

interface RouterState {  
    [actionData](react_router.RouterState.html#actionData)
: null | RouteData;  
    [blockers](react_router.RouterState.html#blockers)
: Map<string, [Blocker](../types/react_router.Blocker.html)
\>;  
    [errors](react_router.RouterState.html#errors)
: null | RouteData;  
    [fetchers](react_router.RouterState.html#fetchers)
: Map<string, [Fetcher](../types/react_router.Fetcher.html)
<any\>\>;  
    [historyAction](react_router.RouterState.html#historyAction)
: [NavigationType](../enums/react_router.NavigationType.html)
;

<any\>;
