### preventScrollReset[](#preventScrollReset)

preventScrollReset: boolean

Indicate whether this navigation should skip resetting the scroll position if we are unable to restore the scroll position

### restoreScrollPosition[](#restoreScrollPosition)

restoreScrollPosition: null | number | false

Current scroll position we should start at for a new view

*   number -> scroll position to restore to
*   false -> do not restore scroll at all (used during submissions)
*   null -> don't have a saved position, scroll to hash or top of page

### revalidation[](#revalidation)

revalidation: [RevalidationState](../types/react_router.RevalidationState.html)

Tracks any in-progress revalidations

=============================

interface RoutesTestStubProps {  
    [future](react_router.RoutesTestStubProps.html#future)
?: Partial<FutureConfig\>;  
    [hydrationData](react_router.RoutesTestStubProps.html#hydrationData)
?: Partial<Pick<[RouterState](react_router.RouterState.html)
, "loaderData" | "actionData" | "errors"\>\>;  
    [initialEntries](react_router.RoutesTestStubProps.html#initialEntries)
?: [InitialEntry](../types/react_router.InitialEntry.html)
\[\];  
    [initialIndex](react_router.RoutesTestStubProps.html#initialIndex)
?: number;  
}

##### Index

### Properties

[future?](react_router.RoutesTestStubProps.html#future)
 [hydrationData?](react_router.RoutesTestStubProps.html#hydrationData)
 [initialEntries?](react_router.RoutesTestStubProps.html#initialEntries)
 [initialIndex?](react_router.RoutesTestStubProps.html#initialIndex)

Properties
----------

### `Optional`future[](#future)

future?: Partial<FutureConfig\>

Future flags mimicking the settings in react-router.config.ts

### `Optional`hydrationData[](#hydrationData)

hydrationData?: Partial<Pick<[RouterState](react_router.RouterState.html)
, "loaderData" | "actionData" | "errors"\>\>

Used to set the route's initial loader and action data. e.g. hydrationData={{ loaderData: { "/contact": { locale: "en-US" } }, actionData: { "/login": { errors: { email: "invalid email" } }} }}

### `Optional`initialEntries[](#initialEntries)

initialEntries?: [InitialEntry](../types/react_router.InitialEntry.html)
\[\]

The initial entries in the history stack. This allows you to start a test with multiple locations already in the history stack (for testing a back navigation, etc.) The test will default to the last entry in initialEntries if no initialIndex is provided. e.g. initialEntries={\["/home", "/about", "/contact"\]}

### `Optional`initialIndex[](#initialIndex)

initialIndex?: number

The initial index in the history stack to render. This allows you to start a test at a specific entry. It defaults to the last entry in initialEntries. e.g. initialEntries: \["/", "/events/123"\] initialIndex: 1 // start at "/events/123"

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

# SessionIdStorageStrategy | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [SessionIdStorageStrategy](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html)
    

Interface SessionIdStorageStrategy<Data, FlashData>
===================================================

SessionIdStorageStrategy is designed to allow anyone to easily build their own SessionStorage using `createSessionStorage(strategy)`.

This strategy describes a common scenario where the session id is stored in a cookie but the actual session data is stored elsewhere, usually in a database or on disk. A set of create, read, update, and delete operations are provided for managing the session data.

interface SessionIdStorageStrategy<[Data](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#Data)
, [FlashData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#FlashData)
\> {  
    [cookie](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#cookie)
?: [Cookie](react_router.Cookie.html)
 | [CookieParseOptions](react_router.CookieParseOptions.html)
 & [CookieSerializeOptions](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html)
 & [CookieSignatureOptions](react_router.CookieSignatureOptions.html)
 & {  
        name?: string;  
    };  
    [createData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#createData)
: ((data: Partial<[Data](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#Data)
 & {  
        \[Key in string | number | symbol as \`\_\_flash\_${[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
 & string}\_\_\`\]: [FlashData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#FlashData)
\[[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
\]  
    }\>, expires?: Date) => Promise<string\>);  
    [deleteData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#deleteData)
: ((id: string) => Promise<void\>);  
    [readData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#readData)
: ((id: string) => Promise<null | Partial<[Data](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#Data)
 & {  
        \[Key in string | number | symbol as \`\_\_flash\_${[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
 & string}\_\_\`\]: [FlashData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#FlashData)
\[[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
\]  
    }\>\>);  
    [updateData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#updateData)
: ((id: string, data: Partial<[Data](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#Data)
 & {  
        \[Key in string | number | symbol as \`\_\_flash\_${[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
 & string}\_\_\`\]: [FlashData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#FlashData)
\[[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
\]  
    }\>, expires?: Date) => Promise<void\>);  
}

#### Type Parameters

*   Data = [SessionData](react_router.SessionData.html)
    
*   FlashData = [Data](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#Data)
    

##### Index

### Properties

[cookie?](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#cookie)
 [createData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#createData)
 [deleteData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#deleteData)
 [readData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#readData)
 [updateData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#updateData)

### `Optional`cookie[](#cookie)

cookie?: [Cookie](react_router.Cookie.html)
 | [CookieParseOptions](react_router.CookieParseOptions.html)
 & [CookieSerializeOptions](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html)
 & [CookieSignatureOptions](react_router.CookieSignatureOptions.html)
 & {  
    name?: string;  
}

The Cookie used to store the session id, or options used to automatically create one.

### createData[](#createData)

createData: ((data: Partial<[Data](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#Data)
 & {  
    \[Key in string | number | symbol as \`\_\_flash\_${[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
 & string}\_\_\`\]: [FlashData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#FlashData)
\[[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
\]  
}\>, expires?: Date) => Promise<string\>)

Creates a new record with the given data and returns the session id.

### deleteData[](#deleteData)

deleteData: ((id: string) => Promise<void\>)

Deletes data for a given session id from the data store.

### readData[](#readData)

readData: ((id: string) => Promise<null | Partial<[Data](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#Data)
 & {  
    \[Key in string | number | symbol as \`\_\_flash\_${[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
 & string}\_\_\`\]: [FlashData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#FlashData)
\[[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
\]  
}\>\>)

Returns data for a given session id, or `null` if there isn't any.

### updateData[](#updateData)

updateData: ((id: string, data: Partial<[Data](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#Data)
 & {  
    \[Key in string | number | symbol as \`\_\_flash\_${[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
 & string}\_\_\`\]: [FlashData](react_router.SessionIdStorageStrategy.html#FlashData)
\[[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
\]  
}\>, expires?: Date) => Promise<void\>)

Updates data for the given session id.

# ShouldRevalidateFunction | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [ShouldRevalidateFunction](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunction.html)
    

Interface ShouldRevalidateFunction
==================================

Route shouldRevalidate function signature. This runs after any submission (navigation or fetcher), so we flatten the navigation/fetcher submission onto the arguments. It shouldn't matter whether it came from a navigation or a fetcher, what really matters is the URLs and the formData since loaders have to re-run based on the data models that were potentially mutated.

*   ShouldRevalidateFunction(args): boolean[](#ShouldRevalidateFunction)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   args: [ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html)
        
    
    #### Returns boolean
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

Interface ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs
======================================

Arguments passed to shouldRevalidate function

interface ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs {  
    [actionResult](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#actionResult)
?: any;  
    [actionStatus](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#actionStatus)
?: number;  
    [currentParams](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#currentParams)
: [Params](../types/react_router.Params.html)
<string\>;  
    [currentUrl](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#currentUrl)
: URL;  
    [defaultShouldRevalidate](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#defaultShouldRevalidate)
: boolean;  
    [formAction](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#formAction)
?: string;  
    [formData](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#formData)
?: FormData;  
    [formEncType](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#formEncType)
?: [FormEncType](../types/react_router.FormEncType.html)
;  
    [formMethod](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#formMethod)
?:  
        | "GET"  
        | "POST"  
        | "PUT"  
        | "PATCH"  
        | "DELETE";  
    [json](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#json)

    [nextParams](react_router.ShouldRevalidateFunctionArgs.html#nextParams)

### `Readonly`data[](#data-1)

data: Partial<[Data](react_router.Session.html#Data)
 & {  
    \[Key in string | number | symbol as \`\_\_flash\_${[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
 & string}\_\_\`\]: [FlashData](react_router.Session.html#FlashData)
\[[Key](react_router.Session.html#get.get-1.Key-1)\
\]  
}\>

The raw data contained in this session.

This is useful mostly for SessionStorage internally to access the raw session data to persist.

### `Readonly`id[](#id)

id: string

A unique identifier for this session.

Note: This will be the empty string for newly created sessions and sessions that are not backed by a database (i.e. cookie-based sessions).

# SessionStorage | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [SessionStorage](react_router.SessionStorage.html)
    

Interface SessionStorage<Data, FlashData>
=========================================

SessionStorage stores session data between HTTP requests and knows how to parse and create cookies.

A SessionStorage creates Session objects using a `Cookie` header as input. Then, later it generates the `Set-Cookie` header to be used in the response.

interface SessionStorage<[Data](react_router.SessionStorage.html#Data)
, [FlashData](react_router.SessionStorage.html#FlashData)
\> {  
    [commitSession](react_router.SessionStorage.html#commitSession)
: ((session: [Session](react_router.Session.html)
<[Data](react_router.SessionStorage.html#Data)
, [FlashData](react_router.SessionStorage.html#FlashData)
\>, options?: [CookieSerializeOptions](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html)
) => Promise<string\>);  
    [destroySession](react_router.SessionStorage.html#destroySession)
: ((session: [Session](react_router.Session.html)
<[Data](react_router.SessionStorage.html#Data)
, [FlashData](react_router.SessionStorage.html#FlashData)
\>, options?: [CookieSerializeOptions](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html)
) => Promise<string\>);  
    [getSession](react_router.SessionStorage.html#getSession)
: ((cookieHeader?: null | string, options?: [CookieParseOptions](react_router.CookieParseOptions.html)
) => Promise<[Session](react_router.Session.html)
<[Data](react_router.SessionStorage.html#Data)
, [FlashData](react_router.SessionStorage.html#FlashData)
\>\>);  
}

#### Type Parameters

*   Data = [SessionData](react_router.SessionData.html)
    
*   FlashData = [Data](react_router.SessionStorage.html#Data)
    

##### Index

### Properties

[commitSession](react_router.SessionStorage.html#commitSession)
 [destroySession](react_router.SessionStorage.html#destroySession)
 [getSession](react_router.SessionStorage.html#getSession)

Properties
----------

### commitSession[](#commitSession)

commitSession: ((session: [Session](react_router.Session.html)
<[Data](react_router.SessionStorage.html#Data)
, [FlashData](react_router.SessionStorage.html#FlashData)
\>, options?: [CookieSerializeOptions](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html)
) => Promise<string\>)

Stores all data in the Session and returns the Set-Cookie header to be used in the HTTP response.

### destroySession[](#destroySession)

destroySession: ((session: [Session](react_router.Session.html)
<[Data](react_router.SessionStorage.html#Data)
, [FlashData](react_router.SessionStorage.html#FlashData)
\>, options?: [CookieSerializeOptions](react_router.CookieSerializeOptions.html)
) => Promise<string\>)

Deletes all data associated with the Session and returns the Set-Cookie header to be used in the HTTP response.

### getSession[](#getSession)

getSession: ((cookieHeader?: null | string, options?: [CookieParseOptions](react_router.CookieParseOptions.html)
) => Promise<[Session](react_router.Session.html)
<[Data](react_router.SessionStorage.html#Data)
, [FlashData](react_router.SessionStorage.html#FlashData)
\>\>)

Parses a Cookie header from a HTTP request and returns the associated Session. If there is no session associated with the cookie, this will return a new Session with no data.

*   Inherited
*   External

# SubmitFunction | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [SubmitFunction](react_router.SubmitFunction.html)
    

Interface SubmitFunction
========================

Submits a HTML `<form>` to the server without reloading the page.

*   SubmitFunction(target, options?): Promise<void\>[](#SubmitFunction)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   target: [SubmitTarget](../types/react_router.SubmitTarget.html)
        
        Can be multiple types of elements and objects
        
        **`HTMLFormElement`**
        
            <Form  onSubmit={(event) => {    submit(event.currentTarget);  }}/>
            
        
        **`FormData`**
        
            const formData = new FormData();formData.append("myKey", "myValue");submit(formData, { method: "post" });
            
        
        **Plain object that will be serialized as `FormData`**
        
            submit({ myKey: "myValue" }, { method: "post" });
            
        
        **Plain object that will be serialized as JSON**
        
            submit(  { myKey: "myValue" },  { method: "post", encType: "application/json" });
            
        
    *   `Optional`options: [SubmitOptions](react_router.SubmitOptions.html)
        
        Options that override the `<form>`'s own attributes. Required when submitting arbitrary data without a backing `<form>`.
        
    
    #### Returns Promise<void\>
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# SubmitOptions | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [SubmitOptions](react_router.SubmitOptions.html)
    

Interface SubmitOptions
=======================

Submit options available to navigations

interface SubmitOptions {  
    [action](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#action)
?: string;  
    [encType](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#encType)
?: [FormEncType](../types/react_router.FormEncType.html)
;  
    [fetcherKey](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#fetcherKey)
?: string;  
    [flushSync](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#flushSync)
?: boolean;  
    [method](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#method)
?: [HTMLFormMethod](../types/react_router.HTMLFormMethod.html)
;  
    [navigate](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#navigate)
?: boolean;  
    [preventScrollReset](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#preventScrollReset)
?: boolean;  
    [relative](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#relative)
?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)
;  
    [replace](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#replace)
?: boolean;  
    [state](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#state)
?: any;  
    [viewTransition](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#viewTransition)
?: boolean;  
}

#### Hierarchy ([view full](../hierarchy.html#react-router.SubmitOptions)
)

*   [FetcherSubmitOptions](react_router.FetcherSubmitOptions.html)
    *   SubmitOptions

##### Index

### Properties

[action?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#action)
 [encType?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#encType)
 [fetcherKey?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#fetcherKey)
 [flushSync?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#flushSync)
 [method?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#method)
 [navigate?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#navigate)
 [preventScrollReset?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#preventScrollReset)
 [relative?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#relative)
 [replace?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#replace)
 [state?](react_router.SubmitOptions.html#state)

Properties
----------

### `Optional`action[](#action)

action?: string

The action URL path used to submit the form. Overrides `<form action>`. Defaults to the path of the current route.

### `Optional`encType[](#encType)

encType?: [FormEncType](../types/react_router.FormEncType.html)

The encoding used to submit the form. Overrides `<form encType>`. Defaults to "application/x-www-form-urlencoded".

### `Optional`fetcherKey[](#fetcherKey)

fetcherKey?: string

Indicate a specific fetcherKey to use when using navigate=false

### `Optional`flushSync[](#flushSync)

flushSync?: boolean

Enable flushSync for this submission's state updates

### `Optional`method[](#method)

method?: [HTMLFormMethod](../types/react_router.HTMLFormMethod.html)

The HTTP method used to submit the form. Overrides `<form method>`. Defaults to "GET".

### `Optional`navigate[](#navigate)

navigate?: boolean

navigate=false will use a fetcher instead of a navigation

### `Optional`preventScrollReset[](#preventScrollReset)

preventScrollReset?: boolean

In browser-based environments, prevent resetting scroll after this navigation when using the component

### `Optional`relative[](#relative)

relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)

Determines whether the form action is relative to the route hierarchy or the pathname. Use this if you want to opt out of navigating the route hierarchy and want to instead route based on /-delimited URL segments

### `Optional`replace[](#replace)

replace?: boolean

Set `true` to replace the current entry in the browser's history stack instead of creating a new one (i.e. stay on "the same page"). Defaults to `false`.

### `Optional`state[](#state)

state?: any

State object to add to the history stack entry for this navigation

### `Optional`viewTransition[](#viewTransition)

viewTransition?: boolean

Enable view transitions on this submission navigation

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

### On This Page

[encType](#encType)
[fetcherKey](#fetcherKey)
[flushSync](#flushSync)
[method](#method)
[navigate](#navigate)
[preventScrollReset](#preventScrollReset)
[relative](#relative)
[replace](#replace)
[state](#state)

# FetcherWithComponents | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [FetcherWithComponents](react_router.FetcherWithComponents.html)
    

Type Alias FetcherWithComponents<TData>
=======================================

FetcherWithComponents<[TData](react_router.FetcherWithComponents.html#TData)
\>: [Fetcher](react_router.Fetcher.html)
<[TData](react_router.FetcherWithComponents.html#TData)
\> & {  
    Form: React.ForwardRefExoticComponent<[FetcherFormProps](../interfaces/react_router.FetcherFormProps.html)
 & React.RefAttributes<HTMLFormElement\>\>;  
    load: ((href: string, opts?: {  
        flushSync?: boolean;  
    }) => Promise<void\>);  
    submit: [FetcherSubmitFunction](../interfaces/react_router.FetcherSubmitFunction.html)
;  
}

The return value of `useFetcher` that keeps track of the state of a fetcher.

    let fetcher = useFetcher();
    

#### Type Parameters

*   TData

#### Type declaration

*   ##### Form: React.ForwardRefExoticComponent<[FetcherFormProps](../interfaces/react_router.FetcherFormProps.html)
     & React.RefAttributes<HTMLFormElement\>\>
    
    Just like [Form](../functions/react_router.Form.html)
     except it doesn't cause a navigation.
    
        function SomeComponent() {  const fetcher = useFetcher()  return (    <fetcher.Form method="post" action="/some/route">      <input type="text" />    </fetcher.Form>  )}
        
    
*   ##### load: ((href: string, opts?: {  
        flushSync?: boolean;  
    }) => Promise<void\>)
    
    Loads data from a route. Useful for loading data imperatively inside of user events outside of a normal button or form, like a combobox or search input.
    
        let fetcher = useFetcher()<input onChange={e => {  fetcher.load(`/search?q=${e.target.value}`)}} />
        
    
    *   *   (href, opts?): Promise<void\>
        *   #### Parameters
            
            *   href: string
            *   `Optional`opts: {  
                    flushSync?: boolean;  
                }
                *   ##### `Optional`flushSync?: boolean
                    
                    Wraps the initial state update for this `fetcher.load` in a `ReactDOM.flushSync` call instead of the default `React.startTransition`. This allows you to perform synchronous DOM actions immediately after the update is flushed to the DOM.
                    
            
            #### Returns Promise<void\>
            
*   ##### submit: [FetcherSubmitFunction](../interfaces/react_router.FetcherSubmitFunction.html)
    
    Submits form data to a route. While multiple nested routes can match a URL, only the leaf route will be called.
    
    The `formData` can be multiple types:
    
    *   \[`FormData`\]\[form\_data\] - A `FormData` instance.
    *   \[`HTMLFormElement`\]\[html\_form\_element\] - A \[`<form>`\]\[form\_element\] DOM element.
    *   `Object` - An object of key/value pairs that will be converted to a `FormData` instance by default. You can pass a more complex object and serialize it as JSON by specifying `encType: "application/json"`. See \[`useSubmit`\]\[use-submit\] for more details.
    
    If the method is `GET`, then the route \[`loader`\]\[loader\] is being called and with the `formData` serialized to the url as \[`URLSearchParams`\]\[url\_search\_params\]. If `DELETE`, `PATCH`, `POST`, or `PUT`, then the route \[`action`\]\[action\] is being called with `formData` as the body.
    
        // Submit a FormData instance (GET request)const formData = new FormData();fetcher.submit(formData);// Submit the HTML form elementfetcher.submit(event.currentTarget.form, {  method: "POST",});// Submit key/value JSON as a FormData instancefetcher.submit(  { serialized: "values" },  { method: "POST" });// Submit raw JSONfetcher.submit(  {    deeply: {      nested: {        json: "values",      },    },  },  {    method: "POST",    encType: "application/json",  });
        
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# NavLinkRenderProps | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [NavLinkRenderProps](react_router.NavLinkRenderProps.html)
    

Type Alias NavLinkRenderProps
=============================

NavLinkRenderProps: {  
    isActive: boolean;  
    isPending: boolean;  
    isTransitioning: boolean;  
}

The object passed to [NavLink](../functions/react_router.NavLink.html)
 `children`, `className`, and `style` prop callbacks to render and style the link based on its state.

    // className<NavLink  to="/messages"  className={({ isActive, isPending }) =>    isPending ? "pending" : isActive ? "active" : ""  }>  Messages</NavLink>// style<NavLink  to="/messages"  style={({ isActive, isPending }) => {    return {      fontWeight: isActive ? "bold" : "",      color: isPending ? "red" : "black",    }  )}/>// children<NavLink to="/tasks">  {({ isActive, isPending }) => (    <span className={isActive ? "active" : ""}>Tasks</span>  )}</NavLink>
    

#### Type declaration

*   ##### isActive: boolean
    
    Indicates if the link's URL matches the current location.
    
*   ##### isPending: boolean
    
    Indicates if the pending location matches the link's URL.
    
*   ##### isTransitioning: boolean
    
    Indicates if a view transition to the link's URL is in progress. See [useViewTransitionState](../functions/react_router.useViewTransitionState.html)
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# RelativeRoutingType | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [RelativeRoutingType](react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)
    

Type Alias RelativeRoutingType
==============================

RelativeRoutingType: "route" | "path"

*   "route": relative to the route hierarchy so `..` means remove all segments of the current route even if it has many. For example, a `route("posts/:id")` would have both `:id` and `posts` removed from the url.
*   "path": relative to the pathname so `..` means remove one segment of the pathname. For example, a `route("posts/:id")` would have only `:id` removed from the url.

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# ScriptsProps | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [ScriptsProps](react_router.ScriptsProps.html)
    

Type Alias ScriptsProps
=======================

ScriptsProps: Omit<React.HTMLProps<HTMLScriptElement\>,  
    | "children"  
    | "async"  
    | "defer"  
    | "src"  
    | "type"  
    | "noModule"  
    | "dangerouslySetInnerHTML"  
    | "suppressHydrationWarning"\>

A couple common attributes:

*   `<Scripts crossOrigin>` for hosting your static assets on a different server than your app.
*   `<Scripts nonce>` to support a [content security policy for scripts](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Headers/Content-Security-Policy/script-src)
     with [nonce-sources](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTTP/Headers/Content-Security-Policy/Sources#sources)
     for your `<script>` tags.

You cannot pass through attributes such as `async`, `defer`, `src`, `type`, `noModule` because they are managed by React Router internally.

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# SetURLSearchParams | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [SetURLSearchParams](react_router.SetURLSearchParams.html)
    

Type Alias SetURLSearchParams
=============================

SetURLSearchParams: ((nextInit?: [URLSearchParamsInit](react_router.URLSearchParamsInit.html)
 | ((prev: URLSearchParams) => [URLSearchParamsInit](react_router.URLSearchParamsInit.html)
), navigateOpts?: [NavigateOptions](../interfaces/react_router.NavigateOptions.html)
) => void)

Sets new search params and causes a navigation when called.

    <button  onClick={() => {    const params = new URLSearchParams();    params.set("someKey", "someValue");    setSearchParams(params, {      preventScrollReset: true,    });  }}/>
    

It also supports a function for setting new search params.

    <button  onClick={() => {    setSearchParams((prev) => {      prev.set("someKey", "someValue");      return prev;    });  }}/>
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# Await | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [Await](react_router.Await.html)
    

Function Await
==============

*   Await<[Resolve](react_router.Await.html#Await.Resolve)
    \>(\_\_namedParameters): Element[](#Await)
    
*   Used to render promise values with automatic error handling.
    
        import { Await, useLoaderData } from "react-router";export function loader() {  // not awaited  const reviews = getReviews()  // awaited (blocks the transition)  const book = await fetch("/api/book").then((res) => res.json())  return { book, reviews }}function Book() {  const { book, reviews } = useLoaderData();  return (    <div>      <h1>{book.title}</h1>      <p>{book.description}</p>      <React.Suspense fallback={<ReviewsSkeleton />}>        <Await          resolve={reviews}          errorElement={            <div>Could not load reviews 😬</div>          }          children={(resolvedReviews) => (            <Reviews items={resolvedReviews} />          )}        />      </React.Suspense>    </div>  );}
        
    
    **Note:** `<Await>` expects to be rendered inside of a `<React.Suspense>`
    
    #### Type Parameters
    
    *   Resolve
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   \_\_namedParameters: [AwaitProps](../interfaces/react_router.AwaitProps.html)
        <[Resolve](react_router.Await.html#Await.Resolve)
        \>
    
    #### Returns Element
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# createCookieSessionStorage | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [createCookieSessionStorage](react_router.createCookieSessionStorage.html)
    

Function createCookieSessionStorage
===================================

*   createCookieSessionStorage<[Data](react_router.createCookieSessionStorage.html#createCookieSessionStorage.Data)
    , [FlashData](react_router.createCookieSessionStorage.html#createCookieSessionStorage.FlashData)
    \>(\_\_namedParameters?): [SessionStorage](../interfaces/react_router.SessionStorage.html)
    <[Data](react_router.createCookieSessionStorage.html#createCookieSessionStorage.Data)
    , [FlashData](react_router.createCookieSessionStorage.html#createCookieSessionStorage.FlashData)
    \>[](#createCookieSessionStorage)
    
*   Creates and returns a SessionStorage object that stores all session data directly in the session cookie itself.
    
    This has the advantage that no database or other backend services are needed, and can help to simplify some load-balanced scenarios. However, it also has the limitation that serialized session data may not exceed the browser's maximum cookie size. Trade-offs!
    
    #### Type Parameters
    
    *   Data = [SessionData](../interfaces/react_router.SessionData.html)
        
    *   FlashData = [Data](react_router.createCookieSessionStorage.html#createCookieSessionStorage.Data)
        
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   \_\_namedParameters: CookieSessionStorageOptions = {}
    
    #### Returns [SessionStorage](../interfaces/react_router.SessionStorage.html)
    <[Data](react_router.createCookieSessionStorage.html#createCookieSessionStorage.Data)
    , [FlashData](react_router.createCookieSessionStorage.html#createCookieSessionStorage.FlashData)
    \>
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

    , [FlashData](react_router.createMemorySessionStorage.html#createMemorySessionStorage.FlashData)
    \>[](#createMemorySessionStorage)
    
*   Creates and returns a simple in-memory SessionStorage object, mostly useful for testing and as a reference implementation.
    
    Note: This storage does not scale beyond a single process, so it is not suitable for most production scenarios.

# Page not found · GitHub Pages

404
===

**File not found**

The site configured at this address does not contain the requested file.

If this is your site, make sure that the filename case matches the URL as well as any file permissions.  
For root URLs (like `http://example.com/`) you must provide an `index.html` file.

[Read the full documentation](https://help.github.com/pages/)
 for more information about using **GitHub Pages**.

# createSearchParams | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [createSearchParams](react_router.createSearchParams.html)
    

Function createSearchParams
===========================

*   createSearchParams(init?): URLSearchParams[](#createSearchParams)
    
*   Creates a URLSearchParams object using the given initializer.
    
    This is identical to `new URLSearchParams(init)` except it also supports arrays as values in the object form of the initializer instead of just strings. This is convenient when you need multiple values for a given key, but don't want to use an array initializer.
    
    For example, instead of:
    
        let searchParams = new URLSearchParams([  ['sort', 'name'],  ['sort', 'price']]);
        
    
    you can do:
    
        let searchParams = createSearchParams({  sort: ['name', 'price']});
        
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   init: [URLSearchParamsInit](../types/react_router.URLSearchParamsInit.html)
         = ""
    
    #### Returns URLSearchParams
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# Form | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [Form](react_router.Form.html)
    

Function Form
=============

A progressively enhanced HTML [`<form>`](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/form)
 that submits data to actions via `fetch`, activating pending states in `useNavigation` which enables advanced user interfaces beyond a basic HTML form. After a form's action completes, all data on the page is automatically revalidated to keep the UI in sync with the data.

Because it uses the HTML form API, server rendered pages are interactive at a basic level before JavaScript loads. Instead of React Router managing the submission, the browser manages the submission as well as the pending states (like the spinning favicon). After JavaScript loads, React Router takes over enabling web application user experiences.

Form is most useful for submissions that should also change the URL or otherwise add an entry to the browser history stack. For forms that shouldn't manipulate the browser history stack, use \[`<fetcher.Form>`\]\[fetcher\_form\].

    import { Form } from "react-router";function NewEvent() {  return (    <Form action="/events" method="post">      <input name="title" type="text" />      <input name="description" type="text" />    </Form>  )}
    

*   Form(props): ReactNode[](#Form)
    
*   **NOTE**: Exotic components are not callable.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   props: [FormProps](../interfaces/react_router.FormProps.html)
         & RefAttributes<HTMLFormElement\>
    
    #### Returns ReactNode
    

##### Index

### Properties

[$$typeof](react_router.Form.html#__typeof)
 [defaultProps?](react_router.Form.html#defaultProps)
 [displayName?](react_router.Form.html#displayName)
 [propTypes?](react_router.Form.html#propTypes)

Properties
----------

### `Readonly`$$typeof[](#__typeof)

$$typeof: symbol

### `Optional`defaultProps[](#defaultProps)

defaultProps?: Partial<[FormProps](../interfaces/react_router.FormProps.html)
 & RefAttributes<HTMLFormElement\>\>

### `Optional`displayName[](#displayName)

displayName?: string

### `Optional`propTypes[](#propTypes)

propTypes?: WeakValidationMap<[FormProps](../interfaces/react_router.FormProps.html)
 & RefAttributes<HTMLFormElement\>\>

*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

# NavLink | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [NavLink](react_router.NavLink.html)
    

Function NavLink
================

Wraps [`<Link>`](react_router.Link.html)
 with additional props for styling active and pending states.

*   Automatically applies classes to the link based on its active and pending states, see [NavLinkProps.className](../interfaces/react_router.NavLinkProps.html#className)
    .
*   Automatically applies `aria-current="page"` to the link when the link is active. See [`aria-current`](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Accessibility/ARIA/Attributes/aria-current)
     on MDN.

    import { NavLink } from "react-router"<NavLink to="/message" />
    

States are available through the className, style, and children render props. See [NavLinkRenderProps](../types/react_router.NavLinkRenderProps.html)
.

    <NavLink  to="/messages"  className={({ isActive, isPending }) =>    isPending ? "pending" : isActive ? "active" : ""  }>  Messages</NavLink>
    

*   NavLink(props): ReactNode[](#NavLink)
    
*   **NOTE**: Exotic components are not callable.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   props: [NavLinkProps](../interfaces/react_router.NavLinkProps.html)
         & RefAttributes<HTMLAnchorElement\>
    
    #### Returns ReactNode
    

##### Index

### Properties

[$$typeof](react_router.NavLink.html#__typeof)
 [defaultProps?](react_router.NavLink.html#defaultProps)
 [displayName?](react_router.NavLink.html#displayName)
 [propTypes?](react_router.NavLink.html#propTypes)

Properties

# PrefetchPageLinks | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [PrefetchPageLinks](react_router.PrefetchPageLinks.html)
    

Function PrefetchPageLinks
==========================

*   PrefetchPageLinks(\_\_namedParameters): null | Element[](#PrefetchPageLinks)
    
*   Renders `<link rel=prefetch|modulepreload>` tags for modules and data of another page to enable an instant navigation to that page. [`<Link prefetch>`](../interfaces/react_router.LinkProps.html#prefetch)
     uses this internally, but you can render it to prefetch a page for any other reason.
    
        import { PrefetchPageLinks } from "react-router"<PrefetchPageLinks page="/absolute/path" />
        
    
    For example, you may render one of this as the user types into a search field to prefetch search results before they click through to their selection.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   \_\_namedParameters: [PageLinkDescriptor](../interfaces/react_router.PageLinkDescriptor.html)
        
    
    #### Returns null | Element
    

### Settings

*   External

# redirect | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [redirect](react_router.redirect.html)
    

Function redirect
=================

A redirect response. Sets the status code and the `Location` header. Defaults to "302 Found".

*   redirect(url, init?): Response[](#redirect)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   url: string
    *   `Optional`init: number | ResponseInit
    
    #### Returns Response

Function redirectDocument
=========================

A redirect response that will force a document reload to the new location. Sets the status code and the `Location` header. Defaults to "302 Found".

*   redirectDocument(url, init?): Response[](#redirectDocument)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   url: string
    *   `Optional`init: number | ResponseInit
    
    #### Returns Response

# replace | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [replace](react_router.replace.html)
    

Function replace
================

A redirect response that will perform a `history.replaceState` instead of a `history.pushState` for client-side navigation redirects. Sets the status code and the `Location` header. Defaults to "302 Found".

*   replace(url, init?): Response[](#replace)
    
*   #### Parameters
    
    *   url: string
    *   `Optional`init: number | ResponseInit
    
    #### Returns Response
    

### Settings

*   Inherited

Function Route
==============

*   Route(\_props): React.ReactElement | null[](#Route)
    
*   Configures an element to render when a pattern matches the current location. It must be rendered within a [Routes](react_router.Routes.html)
     element. Note that these routes do not participate in data loading, actions, code splitting, or any other route module features.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   \_props: [RouteProps](../types/react_router.RouteProps.html)
        
    
    #### Returns React.ReactElement | null

Function Router

# Routes | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [Routes](react_router.Routes.html)
    

Function Routes
===============

*   Routes(\_\_namedParameters): React.ReactElement | null[](#Routes)
    
*   Renders a branch of [`<Routes>`](react_router.Route.html)
     that best matches the current location. Note that these routes do not participate in data loading, actions, code splitting, or any other route module features.
    
        import { Routes, Route } from "react-router"<Routes> <Route index element={<StepOne />} /> <Route path="step-2" element={<StepTwo />} /> <Route path="step-3" element={<StepThree />}></Routes>
        
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   \_\_namedParameters: [RoutesProps](../interfaces/react_router.RoutesProps.html)
        
    
    #### Returns React.ReactElement | null

# Scripts | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [Scripts](react_router.Scripts.html)
    

Function Scripts
================

*   Scripts(props): null | Element[](#Scripts)
    
*   Renders the client runtime of your app. It should be rendered inside the `<body>` of the document.
    
        import { Scripts } from "react-router";export default function Root() {  return (    <html>      <head />      <body>        <Scripts />      </body>    </html>  );}
        
    
    If server rendering, you can omit `<Scripts/>` and the app will work as a traditional web app without JavaScript, relying solely on HTML and browser behaviors.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   props: [ScriptsProps](../types/react_router.ScriptsProps.html)
        
    
    #### Returns null | Element
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

# ScrollRestoration | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [ScrollRestoration](react_router.ScrollRestoration.html)
    

Function ScrollRestoration
==========================

*   ScrollRestoration(\_\_namedParameters): null | Element[](#ScrollRestoration)
    
*   Emulates the browser's scroll restoration on location changes. Apps should only render one of these, right before the [Scripts](react_router.Scripts.html)
     component.
    
        import { ScrollRestoration } from "react-router";export default function Root() {  return (    <html>      <body>        <ScrollRestoration />        <Scripts />      </body>    </html>  );}
        
    
    This component renders an inline `<script>` to prevent scroll flashing. The `nonce` prop will be passed down to the script tag to allow CSP nonce usage.
    
        <ScrollRestoration nonce={cspNonce} />
        
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   \_\_namedParameters: [ScrollRestorationProps](../types/react_router.ScrollRestorationProps.html)
        
    
    #### Returns null | Element
    

##### Index

### Properties

[displayName](react_router.ScrollRestoration.html#displayName)

Properties

displayName: string

# unstable_usePrompt | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [unstable\_usePrompt](react_router.unstable_usePrompt.html)
    

Function unstable\_usePrompt
============================

*   unstable\_usePrompt(\_\_namedParameters): void[](#unstable_usePrompt)
    
*   Wrapper around useBlocker to show a window.confirm prompt to users instead of building a custom UI with [useBlocker](react_router.useBlocker.html)
    .
    
    The `unstable_` flag will not be removed because this technique has a lot of rough edges and behaves very differently (and incorrectly sometimes) across browsers if users click addition back/forward navigations while the confirmation is open. Use at your own risk.
    
        function ImportantForm() {  let [value, setValue] = React.useState("");  // Block navigating elsewhere when data has been entered into the input  unstable_usePrompt({    message: "Are you sure?",    when: ({ currentLocation, nextLocation }) =>      value !== "" &&      currentLocation.pathname !== nextLocation.pathname,  });  return (    <Form method="post">      <label>        Enter some important data:        <input          name="data"          value={value}          onChange={(e) => setValue(e.target.value)}        />      </label>      <button type="submit">Save</button>    </Form>  );}
        
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   \_\_namedParameters: {  
            message: string;  
            when: boolean | [BlockerFunction](../types/react_router.BlockerFunction.html)
        ;  
        }
        *   ##### message: string
            
        *   ##### when: boolean | [BlockerFunction](../types/react_router.BlockerFunction.html)
            
    
    #### Returns void
    
    #### Name[](#Name)
    
    unstable\_usePrompt
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# useActionData | React Router API Reference

*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useActionData](react_router.useActionData.html)
    

Function useActionData
======================

*   useActionData<[T](react_router.useActionData.html#useActionData.T)
    \>(): SerializeFrom<[T](react_router.useActionData.html#useActionData.T)
    \> | undefined[](#useActionData)
    
*   Returns the action data from the most recent POST navigation form submission or `undefined` if there hasn't been one.
    
        import { Form, useActionData } from "react-router"export async function action({ request }) {  const body = await request.formData()  const name = body.get("visitorsName")  return { message: `Hello, ${name}` }}export default function Invoices() {  const data = useActionData()  return (    <Form method="post">      <input type="text" name="visitorsName" />      {data ? data.message : "Waiting..."}    </Form>  )}
        
    
    #### Type Parameters
    
    *   T = any
    
    #### Returns SerializeFrom<[T](react_router.useActionData.html#useActionData.T)
    \> | undefined

Function useBlocker
===================

*   useBlocker(shouldBlock): [Blocker](../types/react_router.Blocker.html)
    [](#useBlocker)
    
*   Allow the application to block navigations within the SPA and present the user a confirmation dialog to confirm the navigation. Mostly used to avoid using half-filled form data. This does not handle hard-reloads or cross-origin navigations.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   shouldBlock: boolean | [BlockerFunction](../types/react_router.BlockerFunction.html)
        
    
    #### Returns [Blocker](../types/react_router.Blocker.html)

# useFetcher | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useFetcher](react_router.useFetcher.html)
    

Function useFetcher
===================

*   useFetcher<[T](react_router.useFetcher.html#useFetcher.T)
    \>(\_\_namedParameters?): [FetcherWithComponents](../types/react_router.FetcherWithComponents.html)
    <SerializeFrom<[T](react_router.useFetcher.html#useFetcher.T)
    \>\>[](#useFetcher)
    
*   Useful for creating complex, dynamic user interfaces that require multiple, concurrent data interactions without causing a navigation.
    
    Fetchers track their own, independent state and can be used to load data, submit forms, and generally interact with loaders and actions.
    
        import { useFetcher } from "react-router"function SomeComponent() {  let fetcher = useFetcher()  // states are available on the fetcher  fetcher.state // "idle" | "loading" | "submitting"  fetcher.data // the data returned from the action or loader  // render a form  <fetcher.Form method="post" />  // load data  fetcher.load("/some/route")  // submit data  fetcher.submit(someFormRef, { method: "post" })  fetcher.submit(someData, {    method: "post",    encType: "application/json"  })}
        
    
    #### Type Parameters
    
    *   T = any
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   \_\_namedParameters: {  
            key?: string;  
        } = {}
        *   ##### `Optional`key?: string
            
            By default, `useFetcher` generate a unique fetcher scoped to that component. If you want to identify a fetcher with your own key such that you can access it from elsewhere in your app, you can do that with the `key` option:
            
                function SomeComp() {  let fetcher = useFetcher({ key: "my-key" })  // ...}// Somewhere elsefunction AnotherComp() {  // this will be the same fetcher, sharing the state across the app  let fetcher = useFetcher({ key: "my-key" });  // ...}
                
            
    
    #### Returns [FetcherWithComponents](../types/react_router.FetcherWithComponents.html)
    <SerializeFrom<[T](react_router.useFetcher.html#useFetcher.T)
    \>\>
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# useFetchers | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useFetchers](react_router.useFetchers.html)
    

Function useFetchers
====================

*   useFetchers(): ([Fetcher](../types/react_router.Fetcher.html)
     & {  
        key: string;  
    })\[\][](#useFetchers)
    
*   Returns an array of all in-flight fetchers. This is useful for components throughout the app that didn't create the fetchers but want to use their submissions to participate in optimistic UI.
    
        import { useFetchers } from "react-router";function SomeComponent() {  const fetchers = useFetchers();  fetchers[0].formData; // FormData  fetchers[0].state; // etc.  // ...}
        
    
    #### Returns ([Fetcher](../types/react_router.Fetcher.html)
     & {  
        key: string;  
    })\[\]
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

# useFormAction | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useFormAction](react_router.useFormAction.html)
    

Function useFormAction
======================

*   useFormAction(action?, \_\_namedParameters?): string[](#useFormAction)
    
*   Resolves the URL to the closest route in the component hierarchy instead of the current URL of the app.
    
    This is used internally by [Form](react_router.Form.html)
     resolve the action to the closest route, but can be used generically as well.
    
        import { useFormAction } from "react-router";function SomeComponent() {  // closest route URL  let action = useFormAction();  // closest route URL + "destroy"  let destroyAction = useFormAction("destroy");}
        
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   `Optional`action: string
        
        The action to append to the closest route URL.
        
    *   \_\_namedParameters: {  
            relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)
        ;  
        } = {}
        *   ##### `Optional`relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)
            
    
    #### Returns string
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# useNavigate | React Router API Reference

*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useNavigate](react_router.useNavigate.html)
    

Function useNavigate
====================

*   useNavigate(): [NavigateFunction](../interfaces/react_router.NavigateFunction.html)
    [](#useNavigate)
    
*   Returns a function that lets you navigate programmatically in the browser in response to user interactions or effects.
    
        import { useNavigate } from "react-router";function SomeComponent() {  let navigate = useNavigate();  return (    <button      onClick={() => {        navigate(-1);      }}    />  );}
        
    
    It's often better to use [redirect](react_router.redirect.html)
     in [actions](../interfaces/react_router.ActionFunction.html)
     and [loaders](../types/react_router.LoaderFunction.html)
     than this hook.
    
    #### Returns [NavigateFunction](../interfaces/react_router.NavigateFunction.html)

*   External

# useNavigation | React Router API Reference

*   [useNavigation](react_router.useNavigation.html)
    

Function useNavigation
======================

*   useNavigation(): [Navigation](../types/react_router.Navigation.html)
    [](#useNavigation)
    
*   Returns the current navigation, defaulting to an "idle" navigation when no navigation is in progress. You can use this to render pending UI (like a global spinner) or read FormData from a form navigation.
    
        import { useNavigation } from "react-router"function SomeComponent() {  let navigation = useNavigation();  navigation.state  navigation.formData  // etc.}
        
    
    #### Returns [Navigation](../types/react_router.Navigation.html)

# useParams | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useParams](react_router.useParams.html)
    

Function useParams
==================

*   useParams<[ParamsOrKey](react_router.useParams.html#useParams.ParamsOrKey)
    \>(): Readonly<\[[ParamsOrKey](react_router.useParams.html#useParams.ParamsOrKey)\
    \] extends \[string\]  
        ? [Params](../types/react_router.Params.html)
    <[ParamsOrKey](react_router.useParams.html#useParams.ParamsOrKey)
    \>  
        : Partial<[ParamsOrKey](react_router.useParams.html#useParams.ParamsOrKey)
    \>\>[](#useParams)
    
*   Returns an object of key/value pairs of the dynamic params from the current URL that were matched by the routes. Child routes inherit all params from their parent routes.
    
        import { useParams } from "react-router"function SomeComponent() {  let params = useParams()  params.postId}
        
    
    Assuming a route pattern like `/posts/:postId` is matched by `/posts/123` then `params.postId` will be `"123"`.
    
    #### Type Parameters
    
    *   ParamsOrKey extends string | Record<string, undefined | string\> = string
    
    #### Returns Readonly<\[[ParamsOrKey](react_router.useParams.html#useParams.ParamsOrKey)\
    \] extends \[string\]  
        ? [Params](../types/react_router.Params.html)
    <[ParamsOrKey](react_router.useParams.html#useParams.ParamsOrKey)
    \>  
        : Partial<[ParamsOrKey](react_router.useParams.html#useParams.ParamsOrKey)
    \>\>
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

# useResolvedPath | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useResolvedPath](react_router.useResolvedPath.html)
    

Function useResolvedPath
========================

*   useResolvedPath(to, \_\_namedParameters?): [Path](../interfaces/react_router.Path.html)
    [](#useResolvedPath)
    
*   Resolves the pathname of the given `to` value against the current location. Similar to [useHref](react_router.useHref.html)
    , but returns a [Path](../interfaces/react_router.Path.html)
     instead of a string.
    
        import { useResolvedPath } from "react-router"function SomeComponent() {  // if the user is at /dashboard/profile  let path = useResolvedPath("../accounts")  path.pathname // "/dashboard/accounts"  path.search // ""  path.hash // ""}
        
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
        
    *   \_\_namedParameters: {  
            relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)
        ;  
        } = {}
        *   ##### `Optional`relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)
            
    
    #### Returns [Path](../interfaces/react_router.Path.html)
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# useRevalidator | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useRevalidator](react_router.useRevalidator.html)
    

Function useRevalidator
=======================

*   useRevalidator(): {  
        state: [RevalidationState](../types/react_router.RevalidationState.html)
    ;  
        revalidate(): Promise<void\>;  
    }[](#useRevalidator)
    
*   Revalidate the data on the page for reasons outside of normal data mutations like window focus or polling on an interval.
    
        import { useRevalidator } from "react-router";function WindowFocusRevalidator() {  const revalidator = useRevalidator();  useFakeWindowFocus(() => {    revalidator.revalidate();  });  return (    <div hidden={revalidator.state === "idle"}>      Revalidating...    </div>  );}
        
    
    Note that page data is already revalidated automatically after actions. If you find yourself using this for normal CRUD operations on your data in response to user interactions, you're probably not taking advantage of the other APIs like [useFetcher](react_router.useFetcher.html)
    , [Form](react_router.Form.html)
    , [useSubmit](react_router.useSubmit.html)
     that do this automatically.
    
    #### Returns {  
        state: [RevalidationState](../types/react_router.RevalidationState.html)
    ;  
        revalidate(): Promise<void\>;  
    }
    
    *   ##### state: [RevalidationState](../types/react_router.RevalidationState.html)
        
    *   ##### revalidate:function
        
        *   revalidate(): Promise<void\>[](#useRevalidator.__type.revalidate.revalidate-1)
            
        *   #### Returns Promise<void\>
            
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# useRouteError | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useRouteError](react_router.useRouteError.html)
    

Function useRouteError
======================

*   useRouteError(): unknown[](#useRouteError)
    
*   Accesses the error thrown during an [action](../interfaces/react_router.ActionFunction.html)
    , [loader](../types/react_router.LoaderFunction.html)
    , or component render to be used in a route module Error Boundary.
    
        export function ErrorBoundary() {  const error = useRouteError();  return <div>{error.message}</div>;}
        
    
    #### Returns unknown
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

# useRouteLoaderData | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useRouteLoaderData](react_router.useRouteLoaderData.html)
    

Function useRouteLoaderData
===========================

*   useRouteLoaderData<[T](react_router.useRouteLoaderData.html#useRouteLoaderData.T)
    \>(routeId): SerializeFrom<[T](react_router.useRouteLoaderData.html#useRouteLoaderData.T)
    \> | undefined[](#useRouteLoaderData)
    
*   Returns the loader data for a given route by route ID.
    
        import { useRouteLoaderData } from "react-router";function SomeComponent() {  const { user } = useRouteLoaderData("root");}
        
    
    Route IDs are created automatically. They are simply the path of the route file relative to the app folder without the extension.
    
    | Route Filename | Route ID |
    | --- | --- |
    | `app/root.tsx` | `"root"` |
    | `app/routes/teams.tsx` | `"routes/teams"` |
    | `app/whatever/teams.$id.tsx` | `"whatever/teams.$id"` |
    
    If you created an ID manually, you can use that instead:
    
        route("/", "containers/app.tsx", { id: "app" }})
        
    
    #### Type Parameters
    
    *   T = any
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   routeId: string
    
    #### Returns SerializeFrom<[T](react_router.useRouteLoaderData.html#useRouteLoaderData.T)
    \> | undefined
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# useRoutes | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useRoutes](react_router.useRoutes.html)
    

Function useRoutes
==================

*   useRoutes(routes, locationArg?): React.ReactElement | null[](#useRoutes)
    
*   Hook version of [`<Routes>`](react_router.Routes.html)
     that uses objects instead of components. These objects have the same properties as the component props.
    
    The return value of `useRoutes` is either a valid React element you can use to render the route tree, or `null` if nothing matched.
    
        import * as React from "react";import { useRoutes } from "react-router";function App() {  let element = useRoutes([    {      path: "/",      element: <Dashboard />,      children: [        {          path: "messages",          element: <DashboardMessages />,        },        { path: "tasks", element: <DashboardTasks /> },      ],    },    { path: "team", element: <AboutPage /> },  ]);  return element;}
        
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   routes: [RouteObject](../types/react_router.RouteObject.html)
        \[\]
    *   `Optional`locationArg: string | Partial<[Location](../interfaces/react_router.Location.html)
        <any\>\>
    
    #### Returns React.ReactElement | null
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# useSearchParams | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useSearchParams](react_router.useSearchParams.html)
    

Function useSearchParams
========================

*   useSearchParams(defaultInit?): \[URLSearchParams, [SetURLSearchParams](../types/react_router.SetURLSearchParams.html)\
    \][](#useSearchParams)
    
*   Returns a tuple of the current URL's URLSearchParams and a function to update them. Setting the search params causes a navigation.
    
        import { useSearchParams } from "react-router";export function SomeComponent() {  const [searchParams, setSearchParams] = useSearchParams();  // ...}
        
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   `Optional`defaultInit: [URLSearchParamsInit](../types/react_router.URLSearchParamsInit.html)
        
    
    #### Returns \[URLSearchParams, [SetURLSearchParams](../types/react_router.SetURLSearchParams.html)\
    \]
    

### Settings

*   Inherited
*   External

# useSubmit | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useSubmit](react_router.useSubmit.html)
    

Function useSubmit
==================

*   useSubmit(): [SubmitFunction](../interfaces/react_router.SubmitFunction.html)
    [](#useSubmit)
    
*   The imperative version of [`<Form>`](react_router.Form.html)
     that lets you submit a form from code instead of a user interaction.
    
        import { useSubmit } from "react-router";function SomeComponent() {  const submit = useSubmit();  return (    <Form      onChange={(event) => {        submit(event.currentTarget);      }}    />  );}
        
    
    #### Returns [SubmitFunction](../interfaces/react_router.SubmitFunction.html)

# useViewTransitionState | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router](../modules/react_router.html)
    
*   [useViewTransitionState](react_router.useViewTransitionState.html)
    

Function useViewTransitionState
===============================

*   useViewTransitionState(to, opts?): boolean[](#useViewTransitionState)
    
*   This hook returns `true` when there is an active [View Transition](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/View_Transitions_API)
     to the specified location. This can be used to apply finer-grained styles to elements to further customize the view transition. This requires that view transitions have been enabled for the given navigation via [LinkProps.viewTransition](../interfaces/react_router.LinkProps.html#viewTransition)
     (or the `Form`, `submit`, or `navigate` call)
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   to: [To](../types/react_router.To.html)
        
    *   opts: {  
            relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)
        ;  
        } = {}
        *   ##### `Optional`relative?: [RelativeRoutingType](../types/react_router.RelativeRoutingType.html)
            
    
    #### Returns boolean
    
    #### Name[](#Name)
    
    useViewTransitionState
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

Type Alias GetLoadContextFunction
=================================

GetLoadContextFunction: ((event: APIGatewayProxyEventV2) => Promise<AppLoadContext\> | AppLoadContext)

A function that returns the value to use as `context` in route `loader` and `action` functions.

You can think of this as an escape hatch that allows you to pass environment/platform-specific values through to your loader/action.

Type Alias Config
=================

Config: {  
    appDirectory?: string;  
    basename?: string;  
    buildDirectory?: string;  
    buildEnd?: BuildEndHook;  
    future?: \[keyof FutureConfig\] extends \[never\]  
        ? {  
            \[key: string\]: never;  
        }  
        : Partial<FutureConfig\>;  
    prerender?: boolean | string\[\] | ((args: {  
        getStaticPaths: (() => string\[\]);  
    }) => string\[\] | Promise<string\[\]\>);  
    presets?: [Preset](_react_router_dev.config.Preset.html)
\[\];  
    serverBuildFile?: string;  
    serverBundles?: [ServerBundlesFunction](_react_router_dev.config.ServerBundlesFunction.html)
;  
    serverModuleFormat?: ServerModuleFormat;  
    ssr?: boolean;  
}

#### Type declaration

*   ##### `Optional`appDirectory?: string
    
    The path to the `app` directory, relative to the root directory. Defaults to `"app"`.
    
*   ##### `Optional`basename?: string
    
    The React Router app basename. Defaults to `"/"`.
    
*   ##### `Optional`buildDirectory?: string
    
    The path to the build directory, relative to the project. Defaults to `"build"`.
    
*   ##### `Optional`buildEnd?: BuildEndHook
    
    A function that is called after the full React Router build is complete.
    
*   ##### `Optional`future?: \[keyof FutureConfig\] extends \[never\]  
        ? {  
            \[key: string\]: never;  
        }  
        : Partial<FutureConfig\>
    
    Enabled future flags
    
*   ##### `Optional`prerender?: boolean | string\[\] | ((args: {  
        getStaticPaths: (() => string\[\]);  
    }) => string\[\] | Promise<string\[\]\>)
    
    An array of URLs to prerender to HTML files at build time. Can also be a function returning an array to dynamically generate URLs.
    
*   ##### `Optional`presets?: [Preset](_react_router_dev.config.Preset.html)
    \[\]
    
    An array of React Router plugin config presets to ease integration with other platforms and tools.
    
*   ##### `Optional`serverBuildFile?: string
    
    The file name of the server build output. This file should end in a `.js` extension and should be deployed to your server. Defaults to `"index.js"`.
    
*   ##### `Optional`serverBundles?: [ServerBundlesFunction](_react_router_dev.config.ServerBundlesFunction.html)
    
    A function for assigning routes to different server bundles. This function should return a server bundle ID which will be used as the bundle's directory name within the server build directory.
    
*   ##### `Optional`serverModuleFormat?: ServerModuleFormat
    
    The output format of the server build. Defaults to "esm".
    
*   ##### `Optional`ssr?: boolean
    
    Enable server-side rendering for your application. Disable to use "SPA Mode", which will request the `/` path at build-time and save it as an `index.html` file with your assets so your application can be deployed as a SPA without server-rendering. Default's to `true`.
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# RouteConfigEntry | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [@react-router/dev](../modules/_react_router_dev.html)
    
*   [routes](../modules/_react_router_dev.routes.html)
    
*   [RouteConfigEntry](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html)
    

Interface RouteConfigEntry
==========================

Configuration for an individual route, for use within `routes.ts`. As a convenience, route config entries can be created with the [route](../functions/_react_router_dev.routes.route.html)
, [index](../functions/_react_router_dev.routes.index.html)
 and [layout](../functions/_react_router_dev.routes.layout.html)
 helper functions.

interface RouteConfigEntry {  
    [caseSensitive](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#caseSensitive)
?: boolean;  
    [children](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#children)
?: [RouteConfigEntry](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html)
\[\];  
    [file](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#file)
: string;  
    [id](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#id)
?: string;  
    [index](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#index)
?: boolean;  
    [path](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#path)
?: string;  
}

##### Index

### Properties

[caseSensitive?](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#caseSensitive)
 [children?](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#children)
 [file](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#file)
 [id?](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#id)
 [index?](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#index)
 [path?](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html#path)

Properties
----------

### `Optional`caseSensitive[](#caseSensitive)

caseSensitive?: boolean

Should be `true` if the `path` is case-sensitive. Defaults to `false`.

### `Optional`children[](#children)

children?: [RouteConfigEntry](_react_router_dev.routes.RouteConfigEntry.html)
\[\]

The child routes.

### file[](#file)

file: string

The path to the entry point for this route, relative to `config.appDirectory`.

### `Optional`id[](#id)

id?: string

The unique id for this route.

### `Optional`index[](#index)

index?: boolean

Should be `true` if it is an index route. This disallows child routes.

### `Optional`path[](#path)

path?: string

The path this route uses to match on the URL pathname.

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

# react-router-dom | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [react-router-dom](react_router_dom.html)
    

Module react-router-dom
=======================

This package simply re-exports everything from `react-router` to smooth the upgrade path for v6 applications. Once upgraded you can change all of your imports and remove it from your dependencies:

    -import { Routes } from "react-router-dom"
    +import { Routes } from "react-router"
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

# GetLoadContextFunction | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [@react-router/express](../modules/_react_router_express.html)
    
*   [GetLoadContextFunction](_react_router_express.GetLoadContextFunction.html)
    

Type Alias GetLoadContextFunction
=================================

GetLoadContextFunction: ((req: express.Request, res: express.Response) => Promise<AppLoadContext\> | AppLoadContext)

A function that returns the value to use as `context` in route `loader` and `action` functions.

You can think of this as an escape hatch that allows you to pass environment/platform-specific values through to your loader/action, such as values that are generated by Express middleware like `req.session`.

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---

# flatRoutes | React Router API Reference

*   [React Router API Reference](../modules.html)
    
*   [@react-router/fs-routes](../modules/_react_router_fs_routes.html)
    
*   [flatRoutes](_react_router_fs_routes.flatRoutes.html)
    

Function flatRoutes
===================

*   flatRoutes(options?): Promise<RouteConfigEntry\[\]\>[](#flatRoutes)
    
*   Creates route config from the file system using a convention that matches [Remix v2's route file naming](https://remix.run/docs/en/v2/file-conventions/routes-files)
    , for use within `routes.ts`.
    
    #### Parameters
    
    *   options: {  
            ignoredRouteFiles?: string\[\];  
            rootDirectory?: string;  
        } = {}
        *   ##### `Optional`ignoredRouteFiles?: string\[\]
            
            An array of [minimatch](https://www.npmjs.com/package/minimatch)
             globs that match files to ignore. Defaults to `[]`.
            
        *   ##### `Optional`rootDirectory?: string
            
            The directory containing file system routes, relative to the app directory. Defaults to `"./routes"`.
            
    
    #### Returns Promise<RouteConfigEntry\[\]\>
    

### Settings

Member Visibility

*   Protected
*   Inherited
*   External

ThemeOSLightDark

---
